<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨眠門，指煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何隨眠門所惱？謂與諸纏作所依故，及能引發生等苦故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是隨眠門所惱？是指因為有煩惱的種子在阿賴耶識中，作為煩惱現行的依止處，及能引發生、老、病、死等苦。這是被煩惱種子所困擾的原因。只要有煩惱種子在，就有可能現出煩惱，雖然現在沒有，只要境界現前就會現出煩惱，它最厲害的就是能引發生及老病死，三界輪迴的苦果，這是它的嚴重過患。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、由七門2　辰一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由七門，由七門而生煩惱，分二科；第一科標，標示出來。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="47564:5424"></a>又由七門，一切煩惱於見及修能為障礙應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有七種煩惱門，能夠障礙見道及修道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出七門。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p558"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂邪解了故，不解了故，解了不解了故，邪解了迷執故，彼因依處故，彼怖所生故，任運現行故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能夠障礙見道及修道的七種煩惱是：邪解了故，就是錯誤的認識所知事，有種種的見，如薩迦耶見、邊執見及邪見等，名邪解了。不解了故，就是無明，不明白事實的真相，不了解色受想行識五蘊的生滅無常，不明白四諦的道理。解了不解了故，又是明白又不明白，就是懷疑，有疑的煩惱；對四諦、佛法的道理有懷疑，對見道也是一種很大的障礙。邪解了迷執故，包括見取見、戒禁取見等，以及貪瞋慢，由思想上而生起的煩惱，不只有錯誤的了解而且還迷惑。彼因依處故，是指對苦諦與集諦有迷惑，煩惱是苦諦的原因，對苦諦如果有迷惑就會產生集諦，因此苦諦也是生起煩惱的原因及依止處；過去的集諦，是現在苦諦的因，是苦諦的依止處。因及依處是說明苦諦與集諦互為因緣，過去有煩惱造了業，得到果報身的苦果，依止這個果報身又繼續生起煩惱造業，將來還會得到一個苦果，由於苦諦與集諦互為因緣，互為依止處，稱為彼因依處故。彼怖所生故，是指對於滅諦與道諦有迷惑，以為修道證滅後，死了就斷滅了，而心生恐懼，也障礙見道及修道。任運現行故，前面這幾門都是障礙見道所要斷除的煩惱，任運現行是俱生的煩惱，屬於修道所要斷的煩惱。由這七種門，有疑惑的煩惱，會障礙見道，乃至障礙修道，這是將十種煩惱，以另外一種角度分類。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂邪解了故等者：決擇分云：薩迦耶見、邊執見、邪見，此三於所知境起邪了行，於四聖諦迷行轉故。無明一種，是不了行。疑，是了不了行。見取、戒禁取及貪瞋等，緣見為境、見所斷者，彼一切皆是執邪了行。即此一切迷苦、集諦者，是迷彼因緣所依處行。即此一切迷滅、道諦者，是迷彼怖畏生行。即彼一切任運所起修道斷者，是任運現行迷執行。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/59.htm#5428:47570">陵本五十九卷三頁4791</a>）今應準知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈決擇分〉說：薩迦耶見、邊執見、邪見，這三種煩惱於所知境界生起邪執顛倒的解了，於所認知的四諦，生起了迷惑、錯誤的了解。無明，是指不了解四聖諦的道理。疑，是對四聖諦似懂非懂。見取，執著自己認知的邪見為最殊勝、第一、究竟，或者是依見取而生戒禁取，在行為上取著邪戒或禁，及貪瞋等包括慢，緣思想上的錯誤見解為境，是屬於見道所要斷的煩惱，這些都是不如理作意分別而引起的，都是錯誤的執著與顛倒的心行。對苦諦與集諦有迷惑，不了解集諦與苦諦展轉互為因果，這是迷彼因緣所依處行。對於滅諦與道諦有迷惑、不了解產生怖畏，怕入涅槃什麼都沒有了，這是迷彼怖畏生行。一切任運所起修道斷俱生的煩惱，是任運現行迷執行。在〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷59，1948頁也說到這件事，此處應照〈決擇分〉所說可知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅六、煩惱上品相2　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科煩惱上品相，說明上品煩惱的相貌，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何煩惱上品相？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是煩惱的上品相呢？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋2　辰一、標二相</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科標二相，標出二種相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂猛利相及尤重相。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　上品的煩惱相，是指凶暴厲害相及特重相。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p559"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂猛利相及尤重相者：煩惱現行難可制伏，是名猛利。於微劣事現行增上，是名尤重。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　貪瞋癡煩惱現行的時候，很難去控制與調伏它，名為猛利。於小小的事就可以生起很大的煩惱，名尤重相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、舉六種2　巳一、標列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科舉六種，舉出六種相，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出來。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此相略有六種。一、由犯故；二、由生故；三、由相續故；四、由事故；五、由起惡業故；六、由究竟故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱的上品相，要略而言有六種：由犯故、由生故、由相續故、由事故、由起惡業故、由究竟故。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、隨釋6　午一、由犯故</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分六科；第一科由犯故，由犯戒而生上品煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由犯故者，謂由此煩惱纏故，毀犯一切所有學處。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由犯故者，是指煩惱很粗猛，當它現行的時候，使有情不能持戒清淨，而毀犯一切所受的戒律。學處應該包括戒定慧三學，主要是行為會有錯誤，容易犯戒，煩惱現行的時候，會毀犯一切的戒律。佛說不可以殺盜淫妄，不能控制，就會去做一些不如理的事情，這是一種相貌，會犯戒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、由生故</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由生故，由上品煩惱而生欲界惡趣中。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由生故者，謂由此故，生於欲界苦惡趣中。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由受生的緣故，是指由於煩惱的上品相，將來會生到欲界極苦的三惡道中。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、由相續故</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科由相續故，由煩惱相續而成上品煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由相續故者，謂貪等行、諸根成熟少年盛壯、無涅槃法者。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由相續的緣故，是指上品的煩惱相，有猛利尤重的貪瞋癡煩惱，在六根成熟的青壯年身上或是沒有聖道種子的有情身上，一生又一生的相續。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由相續故等者：若貪瞋癡增上補特伽羅，是名貪等行者。若少年位及中年位，是名諸根成熟少年盛壯者。若闕三種菩提種子，名無涅槃法者。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是貪瞋癡猛利尤重的有情，稱為貪等行者。在少年位及中年位的有情，稱為諸根成熟少年盛壯者。阿賴耶識中缺乏聲聞菩提、緣覺菩提和無上菩提種子，稱為無涅槃法者。這是說到哪一類的人會有這種煩惱的上品相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、由事故</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科由事故，由所緣的對象而成上品煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p560"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由事故者，謂緣尊重田，若緣功德田，若緣不應行田而起。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由所緣事的緣故，是指由所緣的對象為父母等尊重福田、三寶等功德福田、或是鰥寡孤獨、貧窮、老人或者小孩子等不應行田而使煩惱成上品相。田，是能生長榖物處，在這裡是譬喻能生、能增長處，指有恩德者、有功德者、或是不應該生起煩惱的弱勢等對象。相對的，對這類對象所生起的煩惱是屬於上品的，而上品煩惱所造的業也是較重的，下面在業雜染中還會說到。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》由事故等者：於父母所及餘尊重，是名緣尊重田。於佛法僧所，是名緣功德田。於餘一切孤苦貧窮等所，名緣不應行田。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對父母與其他應該要尊敬的，比方說叔父伯父等長輩，或者是家族的長老，或地方的長老，應該尊重的沒有尊重，反而生起貪瞋癡等煩惱，就是煩惱的上品相。佛法僧是功德福田的地方，應該恭敬，卻生起煩惱，就是煩惱的上品相。於餘一切弱勢，孤苦、貧窮、老邁、年幼的人，應該幫助的對象、卻生起煩惱欺壓對方，這就是煩惱的上品相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午五、由起惡業故</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科由起惡業故，由上品煩惱生起惡業的造作。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由起惡業故者，謂由此煩惱纏故，以增上適悅心起身語業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由生起惡業的緣故，是指由這類煩惱數數現行，以非常舒適愉悅的心情，發起身業及語業，這種好樂惡業的煩惱很猛利，是煩惱的上品相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午六、由究竟故</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科由究竟故，由軟品對治道斷上品煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由究竟故者，謂此自性上品所攝，最初軟對治道之所斷故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由究竟故，是說這類煩惱的自性很粗、很猛利、很重，上品所攝，必須以軟品對治道才能究竟斷除。煩惱有軟、中、上品，對治道也有軟、中、上品，上品煩惱由於麤猛、具體、明顯易見以最初軟對治道斷除；中品煩惱以中品對治道斷除；軟品煩惱由於細微、不易覺察、隱藏難現，必須以上品強大的對治道才能斷除。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅七、煩惱顛倒攝2　卯一、舉顛倒2　辰一、標列七種</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科煩惱顛倒攝，由顛倒引發的煩惱，分二科；第一科舉顛倒，舉出顛倒，分二科；第一科標列七種，標列出七種顛倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">煩惱顛倒攝者，謂七顛倒。一、想倒，二、見倒，三、心倒，四、於無常常倒，五、於苦樂倒，六、於不淨淨倒，七、於無我我倒。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱顛倒所攝，是指七種顛倒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、想倒，想的顛倒，非理之想。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、見倒，思想上錯誤的執著，即邪見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、心倒，心與貪等煩惱心所相應成顛倒，即妄心邪識。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、於無常常倒，於世間無常之法生起常見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、於苦樂倒，於世間諸苦生起樂見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、於不淨淨倒，於世間不淨法生起淨見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、於無我我倒，於世間無我法生起我見。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼會有煩惱？原來是有顛倒。於一切所知事認識錯誤，違背常道、不順應正理名顛倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、別釋三倒3　巳一、想倒</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋三倒，各別解釋三種顛倒，分三科；第一科想倒，妄想分別的顛倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">想倒者，謂於無常、苦、不淨、無我中，起常、樂、淨、我妄想分別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　想倒，是想心所有顛倒妄想，凡夫心裡有很多的妄想、分別，對於無常、苦、不淨、無我的色受想行識當中，生起常、樂、我、淨的妄想分別。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p561"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》想倒等者：於所緣境無常計常，苦計為樂，不淨計淨，無我計我，取相而轉；是名想倒。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於所緣的境界，無常執著是常的，苦執著是樂的，不淨執著是淨的，無我執著是我的。心裡這樣想，就是取相，心裡不斷的取著常樂我淨的顛倒相，名為想倒。這是根本的顛倒處，見倒及心倒都是依於想倒，有了妄想、分別，接下來就會有見倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、見倒</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科見倒，見解上的顛倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">見倒者，謂即於彼妄想所分別中，忍可欲樂，建立執著。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　見倒，是指此人在妄想所生起的分別中，有深刻認可自己想法的欲樂，以言論宣說建立自己所執著的想法。見，是以慧心所為體，在思想上強烈的執著某些想法，例如執著對常樂我淨的妄想，且深刻認同及歡喜。用言論來建立宣說自己的想法，而且執著，名為見倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》見倒等者：此說一分出家者，由想倒故，能發見倒。即於邪取顛倒四事生邪執著，是名見倒。由執著故，於自心中生邪勝解，是名忍可欲樂。或復為他開示宣說，是名建立。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　通常是指外道的出家人，或是有學問的人，由於有想倒，能引發見倒。即是對於無常計常，苦計為樂，不淨計淨，無我計我，於四種事生起顛倒錯誤的執著，名為見倒。由於執著這樣的思想，在自己心理產生顛倒錯誤、強而有力認識，名為忍可欲樂，還要將這種思想為大眾開示宣說，稱為建立。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、心倒</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科心倒，心的顛倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">心倒者，謂即於彼所執著中貪等煩惱。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　心倒，是指此人在所執著的想倒、見倒中，心與貪瞋癡煩惱心所和合在一起運作。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》心倒等者：此說諸在家者，由想倒故，能發心倒。謂即貪等煩惱倒染心故，是名心倒。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的諸在家的人，包括一般凡夫，因為有常樂我淨的妄想想倒，能引發心顛倒。由貪瞋癡煩惱顛倒染汙內心，名為心倒。有想倒就會有見倒及心倒，見倒通常是指外道的出家人，或比較有學問的人；心倒則包括在家的或者是一切的凡夫。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、煩惱攝3　辰一、標列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科煩惱攝，將十種煩惱攝為三種，分三科；第一科標列，標示列舉出三種。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知煩惱略有三種。或有煩惱是倒根本，或有煩惱是顛倒體，或有煩惱是倒等流。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道煩惱要略而言有三種。有的煩惱是屬於顛倒的根本，就是無明；或有的煩惱是顛倒的體性，如薩迦耶見，邊執見一分，見取，戒禁取，及貪等；或有的煩惱是顛倒的等流，如邪見，邊執見一分，恚，慢，及疑。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p562"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、隨釋3　巳一、倒根本</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋三種顛倒與十種煩惱的關係，分三科；第一科倒根本，顛倒的根本。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">倒根本者，謂無明。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　顛倒的根本，是指無明。由無明不了解事實的真相，生出常樂我淨的顛倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、顛倒體</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顛倒，顛倒的體性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="12149:5470"></a>顛倒體者，謂薩迦耶見、邊執見一分、見取、戒禁取，及貪。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　顛倒的體性，包括薩迦耶見、邊執見一分、見取、戒禁取，及貪這五種煩惱。薩迦耶見是於無我生起我的顛倒；邊執見一分是指常見，本來是無常的，一般人喜歡常而有常倒，這是於無常常倒；見取，執薩迦耶見、邊執見及邪見等為最、上、無上、勝妙、究竟，煩惱是不淨的，顛倒執為清淨，這是於不淨淨倒；戒禁取是依於見取邪執身口的戒禁，執著持牛戒持狗戒等，認為這樣可以生天，這是於苦樂倒；貪是通於不淨淨倒及於苦樂倒，因為貪愛喜歡的境界，執著不清淨的為清淨而引起貪心。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、倒等流</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科倒等流，顛倒的平等流類。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">倒等流者，謂邪見、邊執見一分、恚、慢，及疑。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　顛倒的等流，包括邪見、邊執見一部分、瞋恚、高慢心及懷疑。邪見，依於我見而生，於無我生起我的顛倒；邊執見一分是指斷見，斷見也是常見的等流，執著一邊、也是於無常生起常的顛倒；瞋恨心、高慢心，以及懷疑，這些都是常樂我淨所引起的煩惱，名為倒等流。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、別廣</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科別廣，各別廣泛詳細的解釋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="65206:5474"></a><a name="62184:5474"></a>此中薩迦耶見是無我我倒，邊執見一分是無常常倒，見取是不淨淨倒，戒禁取是於苦樂倒。貪通二種，謂不淨淨倒及於苦樂倒。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此中薩迦耶見是於無我執著為有我的顛倒，邊執見一分是指執著無常為常的顛倒，見取是不清淨的執著是清淨的，戒禁取是於苦執為樂的顛倒。貪心通於二種，包括不淨執著為清淨的顛倒，及於苦執著為樂的顛倒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》當知煩惱略有三種等者：此說貪等十種煩惱略為三種顛倒所攝。一、倒根本攝，二、倒自體攝，三、倒等流攝。如文可知。顛倒體中，邊執見一分者，於邊見中唯取常見，不取斷見，故言一分。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面所說的薩迦耶見等十種煩惱，要略歸納成三種顛倒所攝：顛倒的根本、顛倒的自體、顛倒的等流，如文所說可以了知。在顛倒體這一類中，邊執見的一分，唯取邊見中無常計常的常見，不取斷見，因此說是邊執見的一分。以上是說明煩惱顛倒互相攝屬的關係。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅八、煩惱差別2　卯一、標列</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科煩惱差別，煩惱的差別相，分二科；第一科標列，標示列出二十六種。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p563"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="47478:5478"></a>煩惱差別者，多種差別應知。謂結、縛、隨眠、隨煩惱、纏、暴流、枙、取、繫、蓋、株杌、垢、常害、箭、所有、根、惡行、漏、匱、燒、惱、有諍、火、熾然、稠林、拘礙，如是等類煩惱差別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱的差別有很多種，包括這裡所列出的結乃至拘礙等二十六種，下面分別說明。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、隨釋2　辰一、釋名字26　巳一、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分二科；第一科釋名字，解釋煩惱不同的名字，分成二十六科；第一科結，煩惱又名結，與苦結合。後面〈攝釋分〉卷89，將煩惱分成四十六種，彌勒菩薩將煩惱說的很微細，應該要好好的認識它的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="839:5480"></a><a name="27843:5480"></a>當知此中，能和合苦，故名為結。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當知道煩惱能夠使令身心與苦和合在一起，所以名為結。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能和合苦故名為結者：能生現法身心憂苦，能生當來五趣生等種種大苦，如是一切名和合苦。異門分說：於五種事能和合故，說名為結。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/84.htm#5481:64402">陵本八十四卷十二頁6387</a>）其義應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能使現在的色受想行識，身體有苦，心中有憂，而且能生當來五趣生老病死等種種輪迴生死的大苦，稱為和合苦。在〈攝異門分〉卷84，2522頁有說到：所結事、能結事、罪過事、等流事、趣向事，這五種事能與苦和合，說明為結。應當了知那裏所說的義理。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、縛</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科縛，煩惱又名縛，像一條繩子，繫縛著有情，使令難以解脫。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">令於善行不隨所欲，故名為縛。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱令於施戒修等善行，不能隨心所欲而轉，所以稱為縛。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》令於善行至故名為縛者：謂依三受起貪瞋癡，於善方便不得自在，故名為縛。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於有情在樂受、苦受、捨受，三受上會生起貪瞋癡，對於善法的方便，不能自在，因此說名為縛。善法方便包括誦經、禮佛、出家、修止觀等這些事情。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、隨眠</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科隨眠，煩惱又名隨眠，指隨逐於心的種子。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p564"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一切世間增上種子之所隨逐，故名隨眠。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　使令有情隨逐生死流轉於世間的強而有力的煩惱種子，稱為隨眠。煩惱稱為隨眠，也稱為麤重，使得心沒有堪能性修習善法；如果是果報性的無記，與其餘無記品，不能很明顯的記別善惡，於修善法力量薄弱稱為麤重，不稱隨眠；窺基大師說：有漏善法因為有煩惱種子未斷，有隱隱然的煩惱在影響，雖然修善，也可以稱為麤重。但是本論〈意地〉卷2說善心所生起，是順於解脫的，因此特別強調善法，不是隨眠也不名麤重。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》一切世間至故名隨眠者：意地中說：諸自體中所有種子，若煩惱品所攝，名為麤重，亦名隨眠。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/02.htm#5488:951">陵本二卷二頁112</a>）若諸有情未離欲求，未離有求，未離邪梵行求者，是名一切世間。彼為煩惱麤重之所隨逐，說名隨眠；隨縛義故，微細義故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在〈意地〉卷2，55頁說到，有情的生命體當中，阿賴耶識所含藏的種子如果是屬於煩惱所攝的，稱作麤重，也稱為隨眠。若有情所追求的沒有遠離欲界一切色聲香味觸的欲，或是沒有遠離對色無色界禪定的愛著，或是執著色無色界禪定就是解脫的邪梵行求，這些都在三界以內，名為一切世間。這些有欲求、有求、邪梵行求的三界有情被三界的煩惱子所隨逐，稱為隨眠。隨順繫縛有情、並且非常微細，障礙有情不能修習善法。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、隨煩惱</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科隨煩惱，煩惱又名隨煩惱，指隨順生起煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="28683:5490"></a>倒染心故，名隨煩惱。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱顛倒染汙有情的心，名為隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》倒染心故名隨煩惱者：謂貪瞋癡隨惱於心，令不離染、令不解脫、令不斷障，名倒染心；即由此義，名隨煩惱。更有餘義，謂從煩惱生故，親近煩惱故，說名隨煩惱。今此不說。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　貪瞋癡煩惱隨順惱亂內心，使令有情不能遠離染污的境界，不能解脫煩惱，不能斷除障礙，證得聖道，名為倒染心；由這個道理，名為隨煩惱。還有其他的道理，就是從煩惱所生的，親近煩惱的緣故，也稱為隨煩惱。現在此處不說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳五、纏</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科纏，煩惱又名纏。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="32353:5493"></a><a name="32353:5493"></a>數起現行，故名為纏。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱常常生起現行，因此說名為纏。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》數起現行故名為纏者：修善品時，現起相續，無斷絕義，是名數起現行。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修習布施乃至般若等善品時，煩惱會出現而且相續、沒有斷絕，名為數起現行。在修善法時，若仔細觀察，會發現有很多的煩惱現行，障礙修善法，稱為纏。不能出離三界，是因為被煩惱纏住，煩惱用各種方式來影響內心，使令有情不能修習善法。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p565"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳六、暴流</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科暴流，煩惱又名暴流。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">深難渡故，順流漂故，名暴流。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在煩惱中，猶如在暴流中，很深、很難渡過，只能隨順在暴流裡面漂泊，名為暴流。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》深難渡故順流漂故名暴流者：如暴流水，深廣難渡，能令有情順流漂溺。貪瞋癡等煩惱亦爾，能令有情生死流轉，難得出離。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱很難斷，好像暴流水，一滴接著一滴，一剎那接著一剎那，很深很廣很難渡越，能令有情隨順生死之流漂泊沈溺。貪瞋癡等煩惱也是一樣，能令有情生死流轉，難得出離。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《阿毘達磨大毘婆沙論》卷78說：有一個外道去難問佛陀，他說：大家讚歎你能夠度眾生，你應該替我斷除煩惱才是真的大慈大悲啊！佛陀告訴他一句話：「我於脫汝疑，必無自在力，要汝見勝法，方能越暴流。」佛陀回答：「我沒有辦法度化你對於生死與三寶四諦的疑惑，我只是提供解脫的方法給你學習，你要自己去修習，自己去證得，見到諸法的實相，才能超越三界生死的暴流。」如果可以，佛陀早已替眾生超越了，怎麼會留眾生在這裡呢？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳七、枙</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科枙，煩惱又名枙。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">邪行方便，故名為枙。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱是錯誤的邪行方便，因此說名為枙。卷8，枙是駕車時套在馬頸上的曲木。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》邪行方便故名為枙者：此約前際邪行方便，能令現法生死流轉，是名為枙。障礙離繫，是枙義故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是約過去生有錯誤的行為，使令有情現在在生死流轉，因此說名為枙。煩惱障礙有情遠離三界的繫縛，名為枙義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳八、取</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科取，煩惱又名取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能取自身相續不絕，故名為取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱夠在三界中取得自己下一世的果報體，相續不斷絕，因此也名為取。有取著的意思。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能取自身相續不絕故名為取者：此約現在愛取方便，能令未來生死流轉而無斷絕，是名為取。執取諍根，執取後有，是取義故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面說的是前際邪行方便，這裡是說現在的愛取方便，如果對生命有愛有取，有愛著的心，有取著的行為，能夠取得將來的果報體，繼續在生死中流轉而無斷絕，稱為取。執取煩惱諍論的根本，執取後有的五蘊，是取的意涵。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《大乘阿毘達磨集論》卷4說：取有四種，包括欲取、見取、戒禁取、我語取。執取諍根、執取後有是取義。由貪著諸欲繫縛耽染為因，諸在家者更相鬥諍，這是諍論的根本，是第一取；由貪著諸見繫縛耽染為因，諸出家者更相鬪諍，這是諍論的根本，是後三取。六十二見趣，名見取。各別禁戒多分苦行，是戒禁取；戒禁取所依止薩迦耶見，是我語取。由見取戒禁取，諸外道輩更相諍論；由我語取諸外道輩互無諍論，而與正法者互有諍論。這些執著諍論的根本，又能引取後有苦果異熟，因此說名為取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳九、繫</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科繫，煩惱又名繫。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p566"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">難可解脫，故名為繫。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　被煩惱繫住，難以解脫，因此稱為繫。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》難可解脫故名為繫者：此中繫言，所謂身繫，以能障礙定意性身故。由此為因，令心散亂不得正定，乃至不得離染解脫，證無所作究竟涅槃，是名難可解脫。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的繫，是指身體是一種繫縛，能障礙得到禪定。禪定是意性身，就是意生身，由意所生的身體。由於煩惱使令身體粗重，內心散亂不能得到正定，乃至不能遠離煩惱染污，解脫生死的苦惱，不能證無所作究竟寂靜的涅槃，稱為難可解脫。無所作，是指已證得解脫，得任運清淨，不需要再加功用行努力去斷煩惱了。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十、蓋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科蓋，煩惱又名蓋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">覆真實義，故名為蓋。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱障礙真實的義理，像被蓋住一樣，看不到外面真實的相貌，稱為蓋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》覆真實義故名為蓋者：障諸善法，於所知事令不顯了，是名覆真實義。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　障礙所有的善法，使令對於蘊處界這些所知事不能明白通達，名為覆真實義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十一、株杌</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科株杌，煩惱又名株杌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壞善稼田，故名株杌。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　樹根長在地面上，名株。樹沒有枝，只有樹幹沒有樹枝，名杌。樹根浮在地面上名為株杌。如果農田裡面長了很多一根一根的樹根，就破壞了好的庄稼田而不能耕種。煩惱增長能破壞好的福田，稱為株杌。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《蓮修必讀》卷1普能禪師說：「生滅塵勞是夜叉，因何不發菩提芽，心田不長無明草，性地常開智慧花，一句彌陀融似鏡，六門失守亂如麻，勸君趁早回頭望，苦海滔滔無盡涯。」心田若長無明草，能障礙智慧、菩提，而使苦海無涯。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》壞善稼田故名株杌者：如舄鹵田，有多株杌，不任耕植。煩惱亦爾，能令轉成上品相續起故，能令身心無堪能故，由是說言壞善稼田。即依此義，喻名株杌。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　舄，含有鹽質的土地名舄；鹵，是鹹水；舄鹵田的田地是鹹的。鹹的田會長出很多沒有樹枝的樹幹，不能耕種栽植。煩惱也是一樣，煩惱能令轉成猛利尤重的上品相續，令身心沒有堪能修習善法，因此名為壞善稼田。依這種義理，譬喻名為株杌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十二、垢</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科垢，煩惱又名垢。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p567"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自性染汙，故名為垢。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　污濁、穢惡名垢。煩惱的本身是污濁、穢惡、染污的，因此說名為垢。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》自性染汙故名為垢者：毀犯淨戒，不善防護別解律儀，是名自性染汙。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　毀犯清淨的戒，不能好好的防護別解脫律儀，名為自性染汙。各別所持戒條，能成就各別的解脫，名為別解脫律儀。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十三、常害</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十三科常害，煩惱又名常害。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">常能為害故，名為常害。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱能常常危害有情身心，稱為常害。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》常能為害故名為常害者：依貪瞋癡長時數受生死燒害，是名常能為害。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依貪瞋癡的煩惱，長時一次次的受到生死燒惱為害，說名常能為害。常常為害自己的就是煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十四、箭</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十四科箭，煩惱又名箭。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="34715:5523"></a>不靜相故，遠所隨故，名為箭。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱使令身心生起不寂靜的相貌，長遠的隨逐在身心中，名為箭。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》不靜相故遠所隨故名為箭者：如被毒箭，若未拔時多不寂靜；煩惱亦爾，名不靜相。又彼煩惱未生當生，難可制伏；亦如毒箭既引發已，遠所隨逐，名遠所隨。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同被毒箭所射中，還沒有拔除以前，心裡多數慌張不寂靜；煩惱也是一樣，名為不靜相。又煩惱的種子隨逐於心，遇到境界隨時會現起煩惱，生起來之後很難控制調伏，也像被毒箭射到，受傷之後還常常會發作，有種種後遺症，長遠隨逐身心，名為遠所隨。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十五、所有</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十五科所有，煩惱又名所有。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="30248:5526"></a>能攝依事，故名所有。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱能夠攝受所依的果報體，因此稱為所有。能攝的是貪瞋癡煩惱，所攝的是五蘊果報體。當煩惱充滿內心時，有如掌握了身心的所有權，主導有情的身語意去造業，這種情形下，煩惱名為所有。有情的死生流轉相續，也是因為有煩惱，由愛取有，而在三界中取得下一世的果報。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p568"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能攝依事故名所有者：五取蘊事是名依事。由貪瞋癡為能攝受，是名能攝依事。當知此中極鄙穢義，是所有義。復有餘義，名為所有。謂能障捨故，有戲樂故。如下異門分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/84.htm#5528:64462">陵本八十四卷十四頁6392</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色受想行識五蘊的身心名為依事。由於有貪瞋癡的煩惱，能夠攝受五蘊，名為能攝依事。當知煩惱極為鄙賤污穢，是所有義。還有其他的義理名為所有，指能障礙自己的捨心，其中有戲論、愛樂，使令有情難以捨離。如〈攝異門分〉卷84，2523頁所說及〈攝事分〉卷89，2651頁所說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十六、根</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十六科根，煩惱又名根。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不善所依，故名為根。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱能夠生出不善的芽，是不善的所依，因此名為根。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》不善所依故名為根者：由貪瞋癡廣生無量惡不善行，是名不善所依。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於貪瞋癡煩惱，而生起無量無邊會到三惡道去的惡不善行，名為不善所依。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十七、惡行</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十七科惡行，煩惱又名惡行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">邪行自性，故名惡行。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱能生起邪執行為的自性，因此又名惡行。有煩惱的時候就會有錯誤的行為。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》邪行自性故名惡行者：依諸有情愛味世間所有為因，行諸惡行；或復分別世間怨相為因，行諸惡行；或復執著世間邪法為因，行諸惡行。是故此貪瞋癡名為邪行自性。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止各種有情由於愛味貪著世間種種事物為因，造作很多身語意業的惡行；或是依世間與自己有怨的人，瞋恚分別為因，而造作種種的惡行；或是執著對世間種種錯誤顛倒的看法，愚癡為因，造作種種的惡行。因此貪瞋癡名為邪行自性。錯誤行為的體性根本就是貪瞋癡，因為有貪瞋癡而造作種種錯誤的行為。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十八、漏</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十八科漏，煩惱又名漏。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">流動其心，故名為漏。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱使令有情內心流動在色聲香味觸的境界上不能寂靜、因此又名為漏。能使令已有的功德漏失，也稱為漏。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p569"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》流動其心故名為漏者：謂於彼彼所緣境界心、意、識生，遊行流散，由是發生種種雜染，起身語意三種惡行，是名流動其心。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在種種色聲香味觸所緣的境界、心意識生起，遊行流動散亂動，由此發生種種煩惱雜染，造作身語意三種惡行，名為流動其心，因此又名為漏。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳十九、匱</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十九科匱，煩惱又名匱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能令受用無有厭足，故名為匱。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱使令有情受用境界不能知足，因此又名為匱。《楞伽經宗通》卷3說：煩惱使令有情如飛蠅貪求受用，無厭無足。《佛所行讚》卷5說：「知足常歡喜，歡喜即是法，資生具雖陋，知足故常安。不知足之人，雖得生天樂，以不知足故，苦火常燒心。富而不知足，是亦為貧苦，雖貧而知足，是則第一富。」</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能令受用無有厭足故名為匱者：受用諸欲，不知過患，不求出離，耽嗜堅著，是名受用無有厭足。由是常為貧乏眾苦所惱，是故名匱。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於受用色聲香味觸諸欲時，不知道欲是有過患的，不想出離這些欲，而且還堅固耽著嗜好，名為受用無有厭足。因此耽著諸欲，老是覺得不夠，常常為貧乏眾多苦惱所逼迫，因此又名為匱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二十、燒</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十科燒，煩惱又名燒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能令所欲常有匱乏，故名為燒。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱能令自己想要的東西，常常覺得缺乏不足，因此又名為燒。例如生起煩惱時會使本來想與自己合作的人，因為自己生起煩惱而離開，因此內心常常被煩惱所燒。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能令所欲常有匱乏故名為燒者：謂如非愛合會，所愛乖離，貪求利養等，是名所欲常有匱乏。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的所欲常有匱乏，例如非愛合會的怨憎會，與不喜歡的人在一起；所愛乖離，與所親愛的人，由種種原因而分離甚至死別，及貪求財利供養等，名所欲常有匱乏。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二十一、惱</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十一科惱，煩惱又名惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能引衰損，故名為惱。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱能引發衰敗損壞，因此又名為惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能引衰損故名為惱者：此中衰損，謂愁歎憂苦惱。隨所愛樂若變壞時，是諸有情便為種種愁歎等苦所惱亂故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的衰損，是指愁歎憂苦惱。有煩惱時，會悲戚、哀歎、憂愁、苦惱。所愛的境界如果變壞的時候，有情就為種種的悲愁哀歎等苦惱所惱亂。惱，主要是說壞苦。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p570"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二十二、有諍</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十二科有諍，煩惱又名有諍。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能為鬥訟諍競之因，故名有諍。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱能使自己與他人戰鬥、訴訟、諍論、競賽，因此又名為有諍。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能為鬥訟諍競之因故名有諍者：鬥訟諍競，或依耽著諸欲所起，或依諸見所生，是名鬥訟諍競之因。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　會與他人戰鬥、訴訟、諍論、競賽，或是由於貪愛耽著諸欲的愛煩惱所生起，或是依止種種的諸見的見煩惱所生起，是名鬥訟諍競的原因。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二十三、火</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十三科火，煩惱又名火。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">燒所積集諸善根薪，故名為火。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　善根像木材一樣，有煩惱時就像點了一把火，將所積聚諸善根的功德材薪都能燒掉，因此又名為火。一念瞋心起，百萬障門開。有煩惱的時候，影響善根的力量，就像懺悔能夠影響自己的罪業一樣，煩惱能夠影響已造的功德，而使自己的善根不能相續。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》燒所積集諸善根薪故名為火者：無貪瞋等，名諸善根。先所積集，譬之如薪。煩惱能燒，故名為火。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無貪、無瞋、無癡，名為諸善根。過去所積聚的眾善，好像堆積的木材。煩惱如火能燒，因此稱為火。煩惱像火一樣，會將所有功德燒掉。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二十四、熾然</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十四科熾然，煩惱又名熾然。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如大熱病，故名熾然。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱有如所發的大熱病，因此名為熾然。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如大熱病故名熾然者：如大熱病，燒惱身心；煩惱亦爾，故名熾然。如集論說：為非法貪大火所燒、不平等貪大火所燒，及為邪法大火所燒，故名熾然。（集論四卷十五頁）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如大熱病，會燒惱自己的身心；煩惱也是一樣，因此名為熾然。如《集論》所說：形容煩惱的力量是這麼大，被不合法貪的大火所燒、不平等貪的瞋大火所燒、及邪法的癡大火所燒，所以名為熾然。如《集論》卷4，15頁所說。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p571"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二十五、稠林</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十五科稠林，煩惱又名稠林。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">種種自身大樹聚集，故名稠林。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱能夠取得一期一期的果報身，像很多的大樹聚集在一起，因此名為稠林。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》種種自身大樹聚集故名稠林者：能生種種苦蘊自身，故名為林。由親愛故，彼得增長，展轉滋茂，說名稠林。攝事分說：安立九相後有苦樹，能生當有。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/93.htm#5561:71006">陵本九十三卷五頁7000</a>）其義應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱能招感一期一期五趣苦的果報身，像樹林一樣那麼多，所以稱為林。由於愛著煩惱，使煩惱能夠繼續增長、展轉滋潤茂盛，名為稠林。〈攝事分〉說，依安立九種相說明煩惱能夠生出後有的苦樹，能夠生出當來的生命體。如〈攝事分〉卷93，2740頁所說，準照該處的義理應當了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二十六、拘礙</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十六科拘礙，煩惱又名拘礙。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能令眾生樂著種種妙欲塵故，能障證得出世法故，名為拘礙。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱能令眾生歡喜耽著在種種的色聲香味觸妙五欲中，能障礙證得出世間的涅槃，因此名為拘礙。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能令眾生至名為拘礙者：拘謂拘縛，令不出離。礙謂障礙，令不證得。能令眾生樂著種種妙欲塵故，此釋名拘。能障證得出世法故，此釋名礙。總略而言，不能修善，故名拘礙。如餘處說。（集論四卷十五頁）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　拘，是將眾生拘束繫縛在依處，使令不能出離。礙，是障礙，令不能證得諸法實相。煩惱能令眾生耽著在種種妙五欲中，這是解釋拘。能障礙證得出世間法，這是解釋礙。總體要略來說，障礙不能修行善法，因此名為拘礙。如餘處《集論》卷4，15頁所說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、顯差別2　巳一、標建立</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯差別，顯示煩惱的差別相，分二科；第一科標建立，標出建立差別相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸如是等煩惱差別，佛薄伽梵隨所增彊，於彼種種煩惱門中建立差別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些二十六種煩惱差別，佛陀隨著煩惱與過患力量所增強的地方，在種種煩惱門中，建立了差別，依煩惱的過患與特性來建立煩惱的名字。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、別體相14　午一、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別體相，各別的體相，分十四科；第一科結，說明結的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p572"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">結者，九結。謂愛結等，廣說如前。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　結，是和合苦，有九種。包括愛結、恚結、慢結、無明結、見結、取結、疑結、嫉結、慳結，詳細內涵如前文所說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、縛</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科縛，說明繫縛的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">縛者，三縛。謂貪瞋癡。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　縛，是令於善行，不隨所欲，稱為縛。有貪、瞋、癡，三種縛。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、隨眠</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科隨眠，說明隨眠的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">隨眠者，七種隨眠。謂欲貪隨眠等，廣說如前。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　隨眠，有七種隨眠，包括：欲貪隨眠、瞋恚隨眠、有貪隨眠、慢隨眠、無明隨眠、見隨眠、疑隨眠，詳細內涵如前文所說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午四、隨煩惱</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科隨煩惱，說明隨煩惱的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">隨煩惱者，三隨煩惱。謂貪瞋癡。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　隨煩惱，倒染心名隨煩惱，貪瞋癡能夠顛倒染汙有情的心，稱為三種隨煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午五、纏</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科纏，說明纏的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">纏者，八纏。謂無慚、無愧、惛沈、睡眠、掉舉、惡作、嫉妒、慳吝。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　纏，數數現行名纏，有八種纏：無慚與無愧，障礙持戒清淨；惛沉與睡眠，障礙修止；掉舉與惡作，障礙修觀；嫉妒與慳吝，面對受用財或受用法時，會有慳貪或嫉妒障礙修捨的善法。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午六、暴流等2　未一、舉暴流</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科暴流等，說明暴流的體相，分二科；第一科舉暴流，舉出四種暴流。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="13862:5579"></a>暴流者，四暴流。謂欲暴流、有暴流、見暴流、無明暴流。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　暴流有：欲暴流、有暴流、見暴流、無明暴流，四種。欲暴流，是對欲的貪愛。有暴流，是對色、無色界禪定的貪愛著；見暴流，是對於思想的執著，通常是指外道，執著各式各樣的邪見、邊執見、薩迦耶見；無明暴流，是對於三界所有的無知。通常欲暴流是指在家的或者是凡夫；有暴流、見暴流、無明暴流，是外道的出家人或有學問的人。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、例枙</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例枙，例舉枙暴流。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如暴流，枙亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同暴流，枙煩惱也是如此，邪行方便也是一樣有四種。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p573"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午七、取</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科取，說明取的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">取者，四取。謂欲取、見取、戒禁取、我語取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　取著，也是有四種。欲取，對於色聲香味觸有欲，主要是內心的煩惱欲。見取，是對於思想的取著，有種種的見，執著己見。戒禁取，是對於錯誤、邪執身語行的取著。我語取，外道執著「我」是真實的，而且認為有「我」，就發表出言論，在言論上不斷的說我怎麼樣，我怎麼樣，名為我語取。因為有我執為依止，就有欲取、見取、戒禁取、我語取四種取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午八、繫</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科繫，說明繫的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">繫者，四繫。謂貪身繫、瞋身繫、戒禁取身繫、此實執取身繫。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　繫，四繫，是貪身繫、瞋身繫、戒禁取身繫、此實執取身繫。〈攝事分〉卷87，2598頁，依外道來說明四繫：「又諸外道、於所妄計一切生處，如大自在、那羅衍拏、及眾主等、無量品類，樂生彼處，名貪身繫。於他諸見異分法中，深憎嫉故，名瞋身繫。依於邪願，修梵行故，於同梵行可樂法中，起憎背故；由此二緣，於增上戒學，能為雜染，當知即彼由戒禁取，於增上心學，能為雜染。由此實執取身繫故；於增上慧學，能為雜染。如是四法，能於色身名身，趣向所緣，安立事中，令心繫縛；故名身繫。」相對於外道，一般欲界眾生對於五欲順情等境，心生貪愛，起諸惑業，束縛於身而不得解脫，名貪身繫。欲界眾生對於五欲違情等境，起瞋恚煩惱而不得解脫，名瞋身繫。非因計因，學外道持守牛戒等邪戒，而增長惑業，束縛於身，名戒禁取身繫。此實執取身繫，又名我見身縛，由我見而增長諸惑業，束縛於身，名此實執取身繫。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午九、蓋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科蓋，說明蓋的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">蓋者，五蓋。謂貪欲蓋、瞋恚蓋、惛沈睡眠蓋、掉舉惡作蓋、疑蓋。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　蓋，是指五蓋。貪欲蓋在本論的解釋，是指障礙出家，在家人如果有貪欲則不能出家。瞋恚蓋是指出家以後有錯誤，他人教授教誡自己的時候，內心有瞋心，不接受，名瞋恚蓋。惛沈睡眠蓋，會障礙修奢摩他。掉舉惡作蓋，障礙修觀。疑蓋，障礙對於佛法真實相貌的認識，障礙修道諦及證滅諦；與他人討論佛法的時候，心懷猶豫不能決定，稱為疑蓋。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午十、株杌等2　未一、舉株杌</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科株杌等，說明株杌的體相，分二科；第一科舉株杌，舉出三株杌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="64452:5590"></a>株杌者，三株杌。謂貪瞋癡。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　株杌，壞善稼田名株杌，有三種，即貪瞋癡，名三株杌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、例垢等</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例垢等，例垢等煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如株杌，如是垢、常害、箭、所有、惡行亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同株杌，垢、常害、箭、所有、惡行等這些煩惱也一樣有三種，就是貪瞋癡。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午十一、根</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科根，說明根的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">根者，三不善根。謂貪不善根、瞋不善根、癡不善根。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　根，是指貪瞋癡三種不善根。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午十二、漏</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科漏，說明漏的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">漏者，三漏。謂欲漏、有漏、無明漏。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　漏，有欲漏、有漏、無明漏三漏。欲漏，是心在色聲香味觸外界的欲上面流動，外門流注，稱為欲漏。有漏，是在內門流注，就是在禪定，執著內心的我愛、我見、我慢，我癡，因此難以與聖道相應。無明漏是執著外門流注的欲漏及內門流注的有漏所依止處，因為有無明，才有欲漏、有漏這二種漏。三界中執著色、執著心，都是無明，稱為無明漏。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p574"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午十三、匱等2　未一、舉匱</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十三科匱等，說明匱的體相，分二科；第一科舉匱，舉出三匱。</span></span></span></div>
