<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="11752:5599"></a>匱者，三匱。謂貪瞋癡。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　匱，能令受用無有厭足名匱，有三種，指貪瞋癡，能令受用無有厭足，名三匱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、例燒等</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例燒等，例燒等煩惱。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如匱，如是燒、惱、有諍、火、熾然、稠林亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同匱，燒、惱、有諍、火、熾然、稠林也是各有三種，就是貪瞋癡。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午十四、拘礙</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十四科拘礙，說明拘礙的體相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="28573:5603"></a><a name="59289:5603"></a>拘礙者，有五拘礙。一、顧戀其身，二、顧戀諸欲，三、樂相雜住，四、闕隨順教，五、得微少善便生喜足。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　拘礙，煩惱將有情拘留在色聲香味觸裡面，障礙證得聖道，名拘礙。有五種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、顧戀其身，顧戀愛著自己的身體；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、顧戀諸欲，顧戀愛著諸欲；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、樂相雜住，喜歡與在家、出家眾在一起雜住；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、闕隨順教，闕乏隨順修學聖道的教授教誡；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、得微少善便生喜足，證得少小善法如未到地定等，便歡喜滿足不求上進。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這五種煩惱，稱為五拘礙。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p575"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於彼種種煩惱門中建立差別等者：於中九結、三縛、七種隨眠、八纏、四暴流、四取、五蓋、三株杌、三常害、三箭、三所有、三惡行、三不善根、三漏，皆如攝事分釋。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/89.htm#5605:68157">陵本八十九卷六頁至十二頁6733</a>）四繫差別亦如攝事分釋。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/87.htm#5605:66598">陵本八十七卷十四頁6593</a>）又拘礙者，此說有五，餘處說三，謂貪拘礙、瞋拘礙、癡拘礙。（集論四卷十五頁）體唯有三，義說有五，故不相違。五拘礙中，言闕隨順教者，謂闕隨順定心教誡教授。得微少善便生喜足者，謂於定地諸善得少喜足。餘文易知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在種種煩惱門中建立差別，其中九結、三縛、七種隨眠、八纏、四暴流、四取、五蓋、三株杌、三常害、三箭、三所有、三惡行、三不善根、三漏等，都準照〈攝事分〉卷89，2646頁所解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四繫差別在〈攝事分〉卷87，2598頁也有解釋。拘礙在本論說有五種，在《集論》卷4，15頁中說有貪拘礙、瞋拘礙、癡拘礙三種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　事實上它的根本體性只有貪、瞋、癡三種，開演成五種，雖然說法不同，並不相違。闕隨順教，是對於如何修定，缺少隨順善知識的教授教誡及學習。修定若有少少的相應，就很高興，滿足在那種境界，使自己不能超越。其實不只包括定，應該包括觀也在裡面，不學習佛法，不知道怎麼樣作觀。煩惱使令眾生顧戀其身乃至得微少善便生喜足。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅九、煩惱過患3　卯一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科煩惱過患，說明煩惱的過失災患，分三科；第一科標，標出過患。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="43201:5607"></a>煩惱過患者，當知諸煩惱有無量過患。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱過患，應當知道煩惱有無量無邊的過失災患。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋過患。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂煩惱起時，先惱亂其心，</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱生起時，首先會使內心非常的混亂。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》煩惱起時先惱亂其心者：煩惱自性不寂靜故，於彼起時，令相應心亦不寂靜，是名惱亂其心。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱的特性就是不寂靜，心裡開始不寂靜時，就知道心裡是有煩惱的。煩惱生起時，使令與煩惱相應的心也是不寂靜，名為惱亂其心。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">次於所緣發起顛倒，</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次會使令有情對所緣境有錯誤顛倒的認識。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》次於所緣發起顛倒者：謂於無常苦不淨無我中，起常樂淨我想倒、見倒、心倒故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於所緣發起顛倒，是指於色受想行識、色聲香味觸法、眼識耳識鼻識舌識身識，這十八界中，各式各樣的境界，是無常的、苦的、不清淨的、也是無我的，生起常樂淨我的想倒、見倒、心倒。由於沒有實相的智慧，生起錯誤顛倒的認識，認為一切是常住不變的、是快樂的、是清淨的、是有我的。先有這樣的認識，這樣想就是顛倒，想久了變成一套顛倒的思想，名為見倒。由於見倒碰到境界就會心倒，生起貪瞋癡。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">令諸隨眠皆得堅固，</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱的種子稱為隨眠，隱藏在心中沒有顯露出來，每動一次煩惱，馬上就熏習成煩惱的種子，使得煩惱的種子越來越堅固。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p576"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》令諸隨眠皆得堅固者：於自體中所有煩惱麤重種子，能令轉成上品相續起故；難可破壞，故名堅固。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱生起時，除了擾亂內心，使得對所緣境發起顛倒，又再熏習自體中所有的煩惱麤重種子，使其更為堅固，能使令煩惱轉成更猛利尤重的上品相，並且一次次相續生起；由於難可破壞，所以稱為堅固。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">令等流行相續而轉。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱生起時，同時會引發其他平等流類的煩惱現行相續生起。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》令等流行相續而轉者：諸隨煩惱，煩惱等流，名等流行。展轉引發，名相續轉。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱生起時，例如有貪煩惱還會有其他煩惱跟著生起，這種平等流類的心行，名為等流行。或者煩惱一直相續生起，使令有情再去動身發語造業，也稱為等流行。煩惱生起時就接著會造業，相續而轉，而且展轉的引發，稱為相續轉。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能引自害、能引他害、能引俱害；生現法罪、生後法罪、生俱法罪；令受彼生身心憂苦；</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱生起時：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、能引自害，先傷害的不是他人，是自己；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、能引他害，能夠損害他人，有煩惱時，表現在自己的身語意上，使得他人受到傷害；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、能引俱害，煩惱生起時，內心先被燃燒影響及傷害自己的身體，也傷害他人；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、能生現法罪，使現在的五蘊有罪；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、能生後法罪，由煩惱引發造作諸業，使將來的生命體還受業報的罪過，重一點的業還延續到下一生或後世；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、生俱法罪，現在的生命體有罪，將來的生命體也有罪，例如殺害眾生罪太重，現世被關，下一生墮到地獄，地獄完了去畜生道受報，畜生完了到人間還遭受短命多病的苦報，名生俱法罪；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此有煩惱生起時，會使令身心生起憂愁苦惱。對於能引自害、他害方面，玅境長老說通常都是俱害比較多，傷害自己也傷害他人。譬如心有煩惱時，自己的臉很難再裝出愉快的樣子，他人看到這種表情，也不會開心。反之，像彌勒佛一樣笑嘻嘻的，任何人看了自然也會開心了。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能引自害至身心憂苦者：此中差別，如下業過患釋。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/09.htm#5619:6619">陵本九卷九頁671</a>）唯彼說業所作，此說煩惱所作，是其差別。煩惱為先，方造諸業，是故此說能引自害等。又下異門分亦有解釋。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/84.htm#5619:64418">陵本八十四卷十三頁6388</a>）其義大同。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能引自害至身心憂苦的這一段文，其中自害、他害、自他害、現法罪、後法罪、現後法罪等的差別，在卷9，276頁的業過患中會說到，那裡所說唯指業造作引起的過患，在此說是煩惱引起所作，這是其中的差別。一定是先有煩惱才會造業，根本的問題在煩惱，不在造業本身，煩惱是主動的，造業是被引發的，因此說能引自害等。在〈攝異門分〉卷84，2522頁裡面也是這樣說，意思也大致相同。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能引生等種種大苦；</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱生起時，還會引發：生、老病死、憂悲、苦惱等種種大苦。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能引生等種種大苦者：等言，等取老病死法。五趣流轉，不能出離，是名種種大苦。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　等這個字，包括老病死法。有煩惱就會造業，在人天地獄餓鬼畜生五趣中流轉輪迴，不能出離，受到生、老病死種種大苦。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p577"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能令相續遠涅槃樂；</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　只要有煩惱在，就會使相續的五蘊身心遠離涅槃的寂靜樂。煩惱使得生死相續流轉，在三界中一次次得到新的果報體，不斷的相續。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能令相續遠涅槃樂者：涅槃界中離貪瞋癡，名涅槃樂。若諸煩惱隨附依身，令不速疾得般涅槃，是名相續遠涅槃樂。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在涅槃的境界中是沒有貪瞋癡的，名為涅槃樂。這不是一般的欲樂，也不是禪定的快樂，是勝義的快樂，因此稱為涅槃樂。煩惱依附隨逐於身心中，使令有情不能得入涅槃，名為相續遠涅槃樂。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能令退失諸勝善法；</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱能令有情退失所有殊勝的善法。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能令退失諸勝善法者：定地諸善名勝善法。由煩惱故，令心散亂，已所得定還復退失，是名退失諸勝善法。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　定地各種善法，名為勝善法。有煩惱時，使心散亂，使所得定又會退失，名為退失諸勝善法。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能令資財衰損散失；</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　煩惱生起時，會做出不如理的事情，導致財產衰損流散，乃至生命也有可能喪失。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能令資財衰損散失者：謂由煩惱等起非理作業方便故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　會使得資財衰損散失，是由於隨順煩惱平等生起，不如理作業的方便為因。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">能令入眾不得無畏，悚懼無威；能令鄙惡名稱流布十方，常為智者之所訶毀；令臨終時生大憂悔；令身壞已墮諸惡趣，生那落迦中；令不證得自勝義利。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有煩惱時，能使自己在大眾中，不能無畏、驚悚畏懼、沒有名聲威勢；常常生起煩惱的人，由於造惡業，惡名昭彰到處都會流傳；常被有智慧的人呵斥、毀責；臨命終時會很後悔；往生以後還會墮到三惡道去，生到地獄中；使令不能成就自己出世涅槃的殊勝義利。義，是涅槃。利，是利益，涅槃是可愛的沒有罪的，是有功德的法。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、結</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結說過患無邊。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是等過無量無邊。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因此煩惱的過失是無量無邊的。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p578"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》令不證得自勝義利者：證自涅槃，名之為義；可愛樂故，無有罪故。證功德法，名之為利；究竟勝利，遠離過患故。煩惱障此，令不證得，故作是說。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　證得自己所要成就的涅槃，稱為義。涅槃是可愛樂的，是沒有罪過的，能夠使令自己成就有功德的法，稱為利，合說為義利。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《金剛經》說：「一切眾生我皆令入無餘涅槃，而滅度之」。因此涅槃是眾生最究竟的利益，能遠離過患的，煩惱障礙涅槃，使令自己不能成就，因此這樣說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所有的煩惱中最嚴重、最根本的就是我執，不用他人教導就有俱生我執，凡夫未轉依前，第七識恆與我癡、我見、我慢、我愛相應，第六意識有分別起的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《十住毗婆沙論》龍樹菩薩說「分別若恆有，真實則永無；分別若永無，真實則恆有。」心一生我我所的虛妄分別，有對立的時候，真實義即不能顯現，若遠離我我所的虛妄分別，就能證得第一義諦。如果沒有將薩迦耶見為根本的我執去掉，走到天涯海角，煩惱都是跟著自己的，唯有修習無我觀，才能去除這些煩惱的根本。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　關於義利有幾種解釋：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1.《無量壽經記》卷1：「言義者，謂義利。義利有二，一者虛妄即是世間利，二真實即具出世利。今簡虛妄，故言真實。」義利可以指虛妄的世間利益，或真實的出世利益二種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2.《佛地經論》卷1：「現益名義，當益名利；世間名義出世名利；離惡名義攝善名利；福德名義智慧名利。」現在獲得世出世間的利益名義，當來獲得世出世間的利益名利；或世間的利益名義，出世的利益名利；或遠離惡法名義，攝受善法名利；或福德名義，智慧名利。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是煩惱雜染，由煩惱的自性、分別、因、位、門、上品、顛倒、差別、及過患等九門所做的詳細說明。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、業雜染2　子一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科業雜染，說明業的雜染，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何業雜染？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是業雜染呢？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、釋2　丑一、標列2　寅一、嗢柁南</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出來。又分二科；第一科嗢柁南，以偈頌說明業雜染。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">嗢柁南曰：</span></strong></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　自性若分別　因位及與門　增上品顛倒　差別諸過患</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　偈頌說：「自性若分別；因位及與門；增上品顛倒；差別諸過患」，五字一句，分成四個句子。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、長行</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科長行，以較長的文字解釋偈頌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知業雜染，由自性故，分別故，因故，位故，門故，上品故，顛倒故，差別故，過患故，解釋應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應知業雜染，由：自性、分別、因、位、門、上品、顛倒、差別、過患，九門分別說明。一由自性故，說明業不共於他法的體性；二分別故，分別業有那些種類，三因故，說明造業的原因；四位故，說明業的位階；五門故，說明業門；六上品，說明業的上品相；七顛倒故，說明造業顛倒的狀態；八是業的差別，業有種種各式各樣不同的差別；九過患，造了業以後有很多的過失災患。這是以長行展開偈頌的內容。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、隨釋9　寅一、業自性</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分九科；第一科業自性，說明業的特性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">業自性云何？謂若法生時，造作相起；</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是業的特性呢？當思業生起時，乃心生起造作相。各式各樣的事情都是法，法可以說是總說的，這裡主要是說思業。思業生的時候，內心有所造作，造作主要是第六意識的思心所。造業時，思心所活動的次第是先生審慮思、其次決定思，最後動發思。先對境界開始詳細思惟觀察，稱為審慮思；接下來做出決定，稱為決定思；最後動發身語稱為動發思。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p579"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若法生時造作相起者：此說思業。彼造作相有五種類。一、為境隨與，二、為彼合會，三、為彼別離，四、能發雜染業，五、令心自在轉。如下決擇分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/53.htm#5644:41472">陵本五十三卷十六頁4261</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　造作相起，是說思業。造作的相貌有五種類。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、為境隨與，第六意識思心所去緣慮境界，稱作為境隨與。一般的視而不見、聽而不聞，都是率爾心之後，沒有進一步的尋求心與決定心，因此沒有相續的第六意識生起；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、為彼合會，第六意識尋求決定後，如果是可愛境會想與境界和合；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、為彼別離，如果是不可愛境界，會想與境界別離；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、能發雜染業，由境界進一步生起愛恚的雜染心，由煩惱而引發不善業的造作；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、令心自在轉，通常是指修世間道或世間道成就者，心不受煩惱繫縛，能隨內心的意願，而入世間定或者出世間定。一般沒有修行的人，心受煩惱控制而不自在。然而修禪定或修聖道成功的人，能令心隨智慧行而轉，這是心自在轉。如〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷53，1760頁所說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">及由彼生故，身行、語行於彼後時造作而轉；是名業自性。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於思業生起，身體的動作及語言的表達（思已業），隨後造作活動；名為業的自性。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》身行語行等者：此說身業、語業。入出息風，名為身行。風為導首，身業轉故。身所作業，亦名身行。由愚癡者先起隨順身業風已，然後方起染汙身業。如入出息能起身業，故名身行；如是尋伺與諸語業俱名語行。如下決擇分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/56.htm#5646:44820">陵本五十六卷十八頁4552</a>）此身語行由思動發，故言於彼後時造作而轉。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡是說身業及語業。出入息風，名為身行。另外一種解釋，以風為導首，風以流動為相，身體就能夠動。因為有風大的關係，身體可以做各式各樣的動作；如果風大不調，身體僵直就不能運動。如同出入息能發起身體造業，因此身體造作的業，也名為身行。由愚癡的人先起隨順身業風已，接著才造作染汙身業。心裡有尋伺，就會想說話。名為先故想，想為先故說。想，就是內心有尋伺。尋伺與諸語業是一起的，名為語行。如〈決擇‧五識身相應地意地〉卷56，1865頁中說。身行及語行，是由思業所動發，因此說身語行是思業之後，才開始造作活動，即思已業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《地藏經》說：起心動念無不是罪、無不是業，只要動一個念頭，就是造業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總之：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、業可分為思業和思已業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、思業即意業，包括審慮思及決定思；思已業即身、語業，乃動發思。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、思（心所）涵括審慮思、決定思、動發思。思業以前二者為體；身語業則以後者為體。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、業分別2　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科業分別，業的分別，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">業分別云何？</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是業的分別呢？</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋2　辰一、略標列2　巳一、由差別</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科略標列，要略標示列舉出來，又分二科；第一科由差別，業由二相建立差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂由二種相應知。一、由補特伽羅相差別故；二、由法相差別故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　業的分別有二種相貌可以知道。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由補特伽羅相差別，造業者的差別；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、由法相差別，業本身的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　補特伽羅就是數取趣，一次又一次到三界五趣中去取得一個輪迥的果報體，換句話說就是人、眾生的別名。由於人所造的業不同，表現在人身心上的相貌也有所不同，譬如說造貪、瞋、癡、殺、盜、淫、妄，表現出來的相貌一定是不同的，這是由人的角度來說明這件事。法相差別，是所造業的法相，由法本身的相貌有所不同來說明。總說是由人與法這二角度來說明十善業與十惡業。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p580"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、由性攝</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由性攝，由業的體性是善或是不善所攝。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復二種，即善不善十種業道。所謂殺生，離殺生；不與取，離不與取；欲邪行，離欲邪行；妄語，離妄語；離間語，離離間語；麤惡語，離麤惡語；綺語，離綺語；貪欲，離貪欲；瞋恚，離瞋恚；邪見，離邪見。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由業的體性來說明它所含攝的內容，分成二大種：十善業道及十不善業道。業是一種通道，可以通到善趣或惡趣，造十惡業會通到三惡道去；造了十善業會通到人天去，因此說業是一種道，稱為業道。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　善與不善的十種業道，由身語意的造作，身業有三種，語業有四種，意業有三種，合說有十善業道和十不善業道。身業三種：殺生，離殺生；不與取，離不與取；欲邪行，離欲邪行。殺生是不善業道；離殺生是善業道。不與取是他人沒有布施或捨棄，未經對方同意而取過來，是不善業道；離不與取就是善業道。欲邪行，凡是夫妻以外的不正當的性行為稱為欲邪行，是不善業道；離欲邪行，沒有婚外的性行為，稱為離欲邪行，是善業道。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四種語業：妄語，離妄語；離間語，離離間語；麤惡語，離麤惡語；綺語，離綺語。說不實的話稱為妄語，是不善業道；離妄語是善業道。離間語，所說的話使令對方彼此之間生起怨隙，離間他們的感情，是不善業道；離離間語，沒有說離間語，是善業道。粗惡語；所說的話很粗暴而且很惡毒，是不善業道；離粗惡語就是善業，說的話很文雅柔和，是善業道。綺語，說令人放逸的話，或是沒有意義的戲論，不能引發義利，是不善業道；離綺語是所說的話能引起正念、引發義利，是善業道。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　意業三種：貪欲，離貪欲；瞋恚，離瞋恚；邪見，離邪見。貪欲，有貪心與思俱行時，是不善業道；離貪欲是善業道。有瞋恚與思俱行時是不善業道；離瞋恚是善業道。邪見，錯誤顛倒的見解與想法，還對公眾加以宣說，嚴重影響他人的思想，這是不善業道；離邪見是善業道。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是以所造業的善性與不善性的角度來說明十善業及十不善業。接下來分別說明十善業、十不善業的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、隨別釋2　巳一、補特伽羅相差別建立2　午一、黑品10　未一、殺生攝4　申一、總舉經言</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨別釋，接著各別詳細的解釋，分二科；第一科補特伽羅相差別建立，依人的角度建立業相差別，分二大科；第一科黑品，黑品十惡業，又分成十科；第一科殺生攝，說明殺生者的相貌，又分四科；第一科總舉經言，總相舉出經中所說的話。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">補特伽羅相差別建立者，謂如經言：諸殺生者，乃至廣說。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以人的角度來說明造十惡業時，如經典上形容殺生的人稱為諸殺生者，乃至更詳細的說，以種種的言詞來形容殺生者的相貌。例如殺生者的身體很緊張，心裡很暴惡等，這裡沒有詳細說明，在別釋經句裡會詳細說出殺生者身心的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、別釋經句2　酉一、總句</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋經句，各別解釋經句，分二科；第一科總句，總說的句子。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">殺生者者，此是總句。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　殺生的人這件事，這是總句。殺生者者，第一個「者」是指殺生的人，因為要說明殺生者，先總相標示出來。第二個「者」是形容殺生者的這件事，是語助詞。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、別句3　戌一、顯示加行殺害2　亥一、別釋2　天一、辨相5　地一、最極暴惡</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別句，各別解釋經中說的殺生者的相貌，分三科；第一科顯示加行殺害，顯示造作殺業，又分二科；第一科別釋，各別解釋。又分二科；第一科辨相，說明殺生者的相貌，又分五科；第一科最極暴惡，殺生者最極端、殘暴的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">最極暴惡者，謂殺害心正現前故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　經典上形容殺生者是最極暴惡的人，當他想殺死人或殺死畜牲等，殺害的心思正現在前，顯示最極暴惡的心相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、血塗其手</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科血塗其手，形容殺生者的身相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">血塗其手者，謂為成殺，身相變故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二個相貌是血塗其手。殺生的人充滿著血腥，為了成就殺生這件事，殺生者身體的相貌會有變化。因為殺生要流血，他的手會沾滿血腥。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p581"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、害極害執</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科害極害執，說明所造的殺生業相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="21036:5664"></a>害極害執者，謂斷彼命故，解支節故，計活命故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　害極害執者，這幾個字中，包含三段文義。其中，害，是指殺害生命；極害，是用殘酷的方法分解受害者的支節；執者，是計度執著以殺生為活命的職業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》害極害執等者：斷彼命故，此釋言害。解支節故，此釋極害。計活命故，此釋言執，謂如不律儀者，計屠羊等自活命故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　動手將被殺者的生命殺害，稱為害。極害，將被殺者的肢節一節一節的解下來，稱為極害。計活命故，解釋為執著，如不律儀者執著以殺羊等為存活養命的職業。計，是執著。律，是佛制定不要殺生的軌則；儀，遵守不殺生的戒，身語意依律所制，稱為儀。不律儀的人沒有持戒，執著殺羊，殺豬，殺雞等方式來養活自己。害、極害、執，這三句話形容殺生者的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地四、無有羞恥</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科無有羞恥，指殺生者沒有羞恥心。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無有羞恥者，謂自罪生故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　殺生的人，沒有羞恥心，自己願意造殺生罪，才會去殺生，不以殺生的事是錯的，因此沒有羞恥心。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地五、無有哀愍</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科無有哀愍，殺生者也沒有哀愍心。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無有哀愍者，謂引彼非愛故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　殺生者沒有哀愍心，殺生會引發被殺者不可愛的境界。自己已經造了一個被殺者不可愛的境界，也為自己樹立了新的冤家，將來自己也會被殺，這是無有哀愍者，也是形容殺生者沒有慈悲心的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、破執2　地一、別辨2　玄一、一切有情所2　黃一、敘外說</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科破執，破除執著，分二科；第一科別辨，各別說明，又分二科；第一科一切有情所，於一切有情所，又分二科；第一科敘外說，敘述印度有些外道的主張。破執是針對外道來說的，外道有一種錯誤的想法，認為殺某些眾生可以殺，某些眾生不可以殺，佛特別提出正義，辨明邪正。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">有出家外道，名曰無繫，彼作是說：百踰繕那內所有眾生，於彼律儀，若不律儀。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　印度有些出家的外道，稱為無繫外道，他們這樣說：「百踰繕那內」，就是百由旬，大約1600里範圍內所有的眾生，如果不殺害，就是有律儀，就是持戒的，如果殺害，就是不持戒。如果是1600里外就不在律儀的範圍內，殺生不犯戒，有這樣錯誤的想法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　換句話說，就是比較近的不要殺，比較遠的若殺牠不是不律儀，這是外道的邪見。佛法說所有的有情都不應該殺，不論是近的或是遠的，通通不可以殺。（1由旬＝16里，100由旬＝1600里）</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》百踰繕那至若不律儀者：此計少分應離殺生。謂隨所住處百踰繕那內眾生，於彼不殺成就律儀，若行殺害成不律儀。不遍一切諸有情所。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　外道執著於少部分有情應該遠離殺生。外道認為，隨所居住的地方，於1600里內所有的眾生不殺害，就是有律儀，就是持戒的，如果殺害就是沒有持戒。但是他們不殺生的範圍太小了，這樣說不合道理的。佛在經裡說不殺害眾生是遍一切有情的，不應分別距離的遠近，以此破外道的種種想法。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p582"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、引經破</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科引經破，引用經典所說破斥外道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為治彼故，說如是言：一切有情所。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了對治外道錯誤的思想，經中說：一切有情，都不可以殺害。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、真實眾生所2　黃一、敘外說</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科真實眾生所，說明真實的眾生，分二科；第一科敘外說，敘述外道錯誤的說法。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即彼外道復作是說：樹等外物亦有生命。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無繫外道又說殺生的範圍是：樹等外物也有生命不可以砍伐。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、引經破</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科引經破，引經典上所說破斥邪說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為治彼故，說如是言：真實眾生所。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了對治外道錯誤的思想，佛教說：於有情識的真實眾生所不能殺。不殺生是指不殺害有情識、感受的有情，不是指沒有情識感受的無情。如食用蔬菜，蔬菜、是沒有情識的，不能算殺生；若是將畜牲或人殺死煮來吃，被殺者有情識分別會感覺痛苦，就構成殺生罪。佛說的眾生是真實的眾生所，指有情識的眾生。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、總顯</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科總顯，顯示這一段的義理。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此即顯示真實福德遠離對治，及顯示不實福德遠離對治。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這兩句話是顯示以一切有情所才是真實福德依止處，對有情有慈悲無害心，即遠離了造不善業與對治；並且顯示不殺害無覺受的草木植物等不是真實福德處及遠離不善業與對治。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此即顯示真實福德遠離對治等者：謂如經言一切有情所，意顯一切有情皆應哀愍。由哀愍故，成就真實福德。不應分別或遠離害，或不遠離。由是對治彼第一計，是名顯示真實福德遠離對治。又如經言真實眾生所，意顯樹等外物無愛非愛，於彼無有哀愍可得。雖遠離殺，而不成就真實福德。由是對治彼第二計，是名顯示不實福德遠離對治。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　經典上說的一切有情所，是顯示於所有的有情都應該慈悲、憐憫。由於慈悲憐憫可以成就真實的福德，因此不應該分別眾生距離遠近，所謂近的不殺害、遠的則不限制，這樣可以對治外道的第一種執著，這稱為顯示真實福德遠離對治。又經典上說真實眾生所，是指有情識、有覺受的眾生，意思是顯示樹等外物沒有情識及可愛不可愛的差別，對草樹等沒有哀愍可得，即使遠離砍伐草樹的殺害，也不會成就真實的福德。這是可以對治外道的第二種執著，名為顯示不實福德遠離對治。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p583"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、結意</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結意，結說其中的義理。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是所說諸句，顯示加行殺害。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這一段所說的殺生句子，顯示出殺生者身心在造作殺害眾生的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如是所說諸句顯示加行殺害者：謂從最極暴惡句，乃至真實眾生所句應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些句子包括：最極暴惡、血塗其手、害極害執、無有羞恥、無有哀愍、一切有情所、真實眾生所，這幾句話都在說明殺生者造作殺生的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、顯示無擇殺害</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯示無擇殺害，顯示沒有選擇的殺害。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">乃至極下捃多蟻等諸眾生所者，此句顯示無擇殺害。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　經中說乃至極下捃多蟻等諸眾生所，指殺生的人連最小的生物也要殺害，顯示沒有選擇的殺害。捃多蟻是印度話翻譯過來的，就是螞蟻已經折斷腳了，折腳蟻名捃多蟻；蟻卵也名捃多蟻。殺生者心極殘暴沒有選擇對象，不論是什麼眾生都要殺害。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》無擇殺害者：謂於諸傍生趣所有眾生，乃至極下捃多蟻等行殺害時，無正覺了，無簡擇心，謂此眾生不應殺害，是名無擇殺害。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　殺生者對於畜生道所有的眾生，從身體大的眾生乃至到極細小的螞蟻等，都要殺害，因為沒有正確的覺悟，沒有正確簡別決擇的心：不認為所有眾生都不可以殺害，這種不正心態名為無擇殺害。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、顯示遇緣容可出離</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科顯示遇緣容可出離，顯示若有因緣，遇到好的善知識正確教導，可以出離殺生。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於殺生事若未遠離者，此顯遇緣容可出離。謂乃至未遠離來，名殺生者。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　殺生者若不能遠離殺生事，這句話顯示如果遇到三寶或是善知識的因緣能了知佛法正確的道理，可以出離殺生，但在沒有遇到善知識而出離殺生之前，還繼續殺生，名為殺生者。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p584"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於殺生事若未遠離等者：謂於殺生起過患欲解，起勝善心，若於彼起靜息方便，及於彼靜息究竟中所有身業，是名於殺生事遠離。由聞正法能善領悟，及受淨戒能善防護，於殺生事止息不作，是名遇緣容可出離。若不遇緣，不出離時，彼業現行，名殺生者。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　知道殺生是有過患的，而生起殊勝善良的心，希望停止息滅殺生這件事而去受戒，若有究竟寂靜止息殺業的決定心，不再有身業去殺害眾生，名為於殺生事遠離。由於聽聞正法，而且能圓滿的領悟正法的道理，及受清淨的五戒，能夠圓滿妥善的防護殺生事，使殺生事止息不作，名為遇緣容可出離。殺生者若沒有遇到好的因緣而出離殺業，當殺業現前時，仍舊名為殺生者。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　古時有一個人，很愛護動物，因為以前的人都睡草蓆，身上會有很多跳蚤，他身上長了跳蚤都捨不得殺，當他要換、洗衣服時，就將跳蚤抓出來，換一個地方給牠住，這樣做了一段時間後，就有了好的果報，他所住的地方三天都不長跳蚤。他有這樣的功德，因為不殺害牠們，那些跳蚤也是有感覺，感覺這個人不會殺害牠們，所以牠們也不讓他身上長跳蚤。他的朋友去外地住旅館時，有很多臭蟲跳蚤，都沒辦法解決的時候，就請這個人去他們房間住三日，三日之後就沒有跳蚤。其中沒有說這個人是佛教徒，而是說這個人從小就不殺生，他連很小的蟲也愛護。如果是一般人都會分別是害蟲或益蟲，害蟲就要殺掉，但他不會，他連害蟲也不殺。眾生都是有心識的，每個有情都愛護自己的生命，不殺害牠，牠也是知道的。很多人去放生都有經驗，那些魚、龜等，都會回頭以身相表示謝謝，有時生病的時候，還會回來報恩救護。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、結明略義2　酉一、第一略義</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結明略義，結論說明要略的義理，分成二科；第一科第一略義，第一種要義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此諸句略義者，謂為顯示殺生相貌、殺生作用、殺生因緣，及與殺生事用差別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面諸多文句的要義，為顯示殺生的相貌、殺生的作用、殺生的因緣，及與殺生的事用差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又此諸句略義等者：殺生相貌，配屬別句中初二句。殺生作用，配屬第三句。殺生因緣，配屬四五句。殺生事用差別，配屬後四句；於中初二句是殺生事差別，次二句是殺生用差別故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　殺生的相貌，配屬別句裡的初二句，即最極暴惡與血塗其手，最極暴惡是指內心的相貌，血塗其手是指身相。殺生作用，配屬第三句的害極害執，指殺生的作用，除了斷彼命，還要解肢節，與計活命故：以殺生為活命的職業。殺生因緣，配屬四五句的無有羞恥與無有哀愍，不覺得這件事是不對的，而沒有羞恥心，也沒有慈悲心。殺生事用差別，配屬後四句，其中初二句是殺生事差別。殺生事，指殺生的對象是一切有情所，還有真實眾生所。次二句是殺生用差別，是指無擇殺害及遇緣容可出離。這是第一種要義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、第二略義</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二略義，第二種要略的義理。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又略義者，謂為顯示殺生如實、殺生差別、殺所殺生、名殺生者。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又第二種要義，是為顯示殺生如實：於一切有情所不應殺生；殺生差別：殺生的對象是指有情識的真實眾生所；殺所殺生：指無選擇的殺害一切眾生；名殺生者：未遇三寶受戒因緣前，殺生現行名殺生者。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又略義等者：於前殺生事用差別中，如次別配四句應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於前所說殺生事用差別中，如其次第各別配合四句解釋應當了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申四、簡非法相</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科簡非法相，簡別不是開顯殺生法相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此諸句，顯能殺生補特伽羅相，非顯殺生法相。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的眾多句子，是顯示能殺生的人的相貌，而不是顯示殺生這件事的法相。先以人的角度來說明殺生，殺生法的相貌，後面還會再詳細說明。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、不與取攝3　申一、釋經句2　酉一、總句</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不與取攝，說明不與取者的相貌。分三科；第一科釋經句，解釋經中的文句，又分二科；第一科總句，總說句。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p585"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，不與取者者，此是總句。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，不與取的人這件事，這是總說句。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、別句14　戌一、於他所有</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別句，以各別句說明不與取，分十四科；第一科於他所有，屬於他人之物。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="47999:5706"></a>於他所有者，謂他所攝財穀等事。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於他人所有的，屬於他人的財產或者稻穀等財物。他人沒有給，自己不告而取就成為偷盜了。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂他所攝財穀等事者：謂諸珍寶，或金或銀，或諸衣服，或諸什物，或香或鬘，如是等類名之為財。謂諸所有可食可飲，大麥、小麥、稻穀、粟穀、糜黍、胡麻、大小豆等，甘蔗、葡萄、乳酪、果汁種種漿飲，如是等類名之為穀。如是財穀無情數攝。等言，等取所餘有情數物，謂或妻子、奴婢、作使，或象、馬、豬、牛、羊、雞、鴨、駝、騾等類應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　他所攝財穀等事，指各種珍寶，或是金、銀、衣服、雜物、香、或者是鬘，鬘就是花鬘等，這類稱為財。他人所有的穀，包括可以吃的可以喝的，大麥、小麥、稻穀、粟穀、糜黍、胡麻、大小豆等，甘蔗、葡萄、乳酪、果汁等類名為穀或飲料，這些是屬於財穀類無情物所攝。這裡的「等」，是包括其他的有情數，包括他人的親人及所養的動物，如妻子，孩子，或者傭人等，或者是他人的象、馬、豬、牛、羊、雞、鴨、駝、騾等類應該知道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、若在聚落</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科若在聚落，於聚落積集、移轉。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若在聚落者，謂即彼事於聚落中，若積集、若移轉。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若在聚落，是指在多人居住的聚落中，將他人的財穀等無情物積集在一起、或將屬於他人的妻子，奴婢等有情移轉至別的處所，都是不與取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於聚落中若積集若移轉者：此中積集，謂於無情數物，若財若穀。移轉，謂於有情數物。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在這些無情物或有情物之中，積集，是指無情數物的財或穀。移轉，是指有情數物。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、若閑靜處</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科若閑靜處，於閑靜處積聚、移轉。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p586"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若閑靜處者，謂即彼事於閑靜處，若生、若集，或復移轉。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在一些比較清靜的地方，名閑靜處。在清靜人少的地方，將他人的穀物移轉至此、或將他人的財產等積聚於此，或將有情移轉至此，都稱為不與取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於閑靜處若生若集等者：此中生言，謂於穀物。集與移轉如前說。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡的「生」，是指生長的榖物。積聚與移轉，如前所說。若是去國家公園或者去海邊遊玩，應該不可以將那裡的草木或者是石頭拿回來，因為那些物還是有所有權的，這一點很多人都會疏忽。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、即此名為可盜物數</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科即此名為可盜物數，不與、不捨、不棄名可被偷盜的物品。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即此名為可盜物數者，謂所不與、不捨、不棄物。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　名為可被偷盜成為不與取的物，是指物主沒有布施出來，沒有捨給大眾、沒有丟掉、放棄所有權的物品。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌五、若自執受</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科若自執受，若是自己執持受用。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若自執受者，謂執為己有。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若將他人東西拿來自己執持受用，認為是自己的，這樣也是不與取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌六、不與而取</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科不與而取，偷盜的行為。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不與而取者，謂彼或時資具闕少，執為己有。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不與而取，可能是因為缺少資具，而將他人的財物拿來當作自己的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌七、不與而樂</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科不與而樂，以偷盜為樂。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不與而樂者，謂樂受行偷盜事業。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　不與而樂，是指歡喜去拿他人的東西，以偷盜為樂。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌八、於所不與不捨不棄而生希望2　亥一、牒經句</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科於所不與不捨不棄而生希望，於偷盜物生貪，分二科；第一科牒經句，表明經中所說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於所不與、不捨、不棄而生希望者，</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對他人擁有的，沒有要布施、捨出、或放棄的物品，心裡生起想要的希望，這樣也是不與取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、釋其義2　天一、釋希望</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋其義，解釋不與取的義理，分二科；第一科釋希望，解釋內心的希望。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p587"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂劫盜他欲為己有。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於他人不與、不捨、不棄的物品，心想將它偷取過來，及占為己有，這是二種心相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、釋不與等3　地一、不與</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋不與等，說明幾種不與取的情況，分三科；第一科不與，說明不與而取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若彼物主非先所與，如酬債法，是名不與。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若物主並沒有要給與，而想要此物的人，以強迫的手段取得，猶如物主所欠債未還，將取得此物方式，如同酬還債務，名為不與。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》非先所與如酬債法者：謂非物主先意欲與，是名非先所與。他生希望，強索而與，是名為酬債法。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　物主沒有想要給與，名為非先所與。但另一個人生起要得到它的希望，強迫物主要給他，名為如酬債法。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、不捨</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不捨，說明不捨而取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若彼物主於彼取者而不捨與，是名不捨。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若物主對於來強迫取走己物的人，並沒有要捨出給與對方，是名為不捨，這也算偷盜罪。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、不棄</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科不棄，說明不棄而取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若彼物主於諸眾生不隨所欲受用而棄，是名不棄。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若物主對於大眾，沒有想要隨他人所想受用而放棄此物，名為不棄。通常布施與捨都是有特定對象的。棄，則是對大眾，沒有特定對象。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌九、自為而取</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科自為而取，自己主動取走。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自為而取者，謂不與而取故，及不與而樂故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　自己逕行取得，包括未經他人同意給與而自行取得，及歡喜去偷盜取得。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌十、饕餮而取</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科饕餮而取，貪心而取。饕餮是貪財、貪食、貪心的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="48390:5738"></a>饕餮而取者，謂所不與、不捨、不棄而希望故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　饕餮而取，是物主沒有答應給與，沒有捨給對方，也沒有說要放棄所有權，卻在心裡生起極大的貪心而去取得。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p588"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌十一、不清而取</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科不清而取，沒有澄清所競物而取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不清而取者，謂於所競物為他所勝，不清雪故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有諍執的物品，稱為所競物。不清而取，是指於所諍執原屬於自己的物品，但是競諍後為他人所勝，對方贏了，自己不去澄清說明，就自行拿走，稱為不清而取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》不清而取等者：謂自所攝財穀等事為他競諍，名所競物。若他得勝，自不清雪，取為己有，是名不清而取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　本來是自己的財物、穀物、自己的人等，可是他人來競諍，對方也想要得到，稱為所競物。結果他人贏了，自己沒有去澄清，就拿過來受用，稱為不清而取。沒有清白的拿到此物，會被他人認為偷或盜，雖然這是自己的，但是沒有說清楚就去取得也不可以。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌十二、不淨而取</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科不淨而取，不是用清淨的方式取得。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不淨而取者，謂雖勝他，而為過失垢所染故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這件事與前一種狀況剛好相反。不淨而取，雖然在競諍時勝了他人，但是所取得的方式是有瑕疵、有雜染過失的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》不淨而取等者：於他所攝財穀等事，自與他競，雖能勝他，取為己有，然有過失，故名不淨而取。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　他人所擁有的財產或穀物等，並不是屬於自己的，可是和物主諍執時贏過他，取為己有，這種取得的方式有不清淨的過失。名為不淨而取。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌十三、有罪而取</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十三科有罪而取，取得的方式是有罪的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">有罪而取者，謂能攝受現法後法非愛果故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有罪而取，以有罪的偷盜方式取得的，是指偷盜之後會受到現世及後世不可愛的果報。現世及後世的果報會有貧窮，資具缺乏的苦惱，雖然從早到晚很努力很辛苦，也是賺不到錢，偷盜的罪業，會使令資財匱乏。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌十四、於不與取若未遠離2　亥一、準前說</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十四科於不與取若未遠離，於偷盜事有沒有遠離的因緣，分二科；第一科準前說，依前面說的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於不與取若未遠離者，如前殺生相說應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果對於偷盜事沒有遠離，如同前面所說殺生相的情況，若有遇到好的因緣學習佛法，則可以出離這種惡不善法，否則還是會偷盜，偷盜現行時，名不與取者。如果有學習佛法，就會知道這麼微細，連自然環境中屬於政府的，有所有權的，都不可以隨便拿。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、例所餘</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例所餘，推例其他的業道。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p589"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所餘業道亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除了這裡所說的殺生業、偷盜業之外，其他的業道也是同樣的遇緣容可出離。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、明略義</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明略義，要略說明其中的義理。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中略義者，謂由盜此故成不與取、若於是處如其差別、如實劫盜、由劫盜故得此過失，是名總義。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中要略的義理是：由於偷盜而成立不與取的罪業；若在聚落處及閑靜處的差別；真實劫盜的可盜物數、若自執受不與而取、不與而樂、於所不與不捨不棄而生希望、自為而取、饕餮而取；由於劫盜因此得到這種過失的不清而取、不淨而取、有罪而取、於不與取若未遠離，這是總義。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此中略義等者：由盜此故成不與取，配屬別句中第一句。若於是處如其差別，配屬次二句。如實劫盜，配屬次七句。由劫盜故得此過失，配屬後四句應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其中的要義是：由盜此故成不與取，配屬別句中第一句的「於他所有」。若於是處如其差別，配屬次二句的「在聚落或閑靜處」。如實劫盜，配屬次七句的「可盜物數、若自執受不與而取、不與而樂、於所不與不捨不棄而生希望、自為而取、饕餮而取」。由劫盜故得此過失，配屬後四句的「不清而取，不淨而取，有罪而取，於不與取若未遠離」，應該要了解。</span></span></span></div>
