<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、簡法相2　酉一、正明建立</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科簡法相，簡別不是不與取法相，分二科；第一科正明建立，正確明白的建立造業者的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又此中亦顯不與取者相，非不與取法相。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又這裡顯示的是不與取「人」的相貌，不是不與取「法」的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、兼例所餘</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科兼例所餘，除了不與取之外，也顯示列出其他的罪業。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知餘亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應知除了不與取偷盜業之外，其他的罪業也是一樣，都是在形容造業「人」的相貌，不是在說造業的「法」相。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、欲邪行攝2　申一、總句</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科欲邪行攝，欲邪行者所攝的相貌，分二科；第一科總句，總說句。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，欲邪行者者，此是總句。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　再說，欲邪行的人這件事，這是總說句。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p590"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、別句2　酉一、釋經句2　戌一、初三句2　亥一、別釋相3　天一、於諸父母等所守護5　地一、父母守護</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別句，各別說明的句子，分二科；第一科釋經句，解釋經中的句子，又分二科；第一科初三句，十句中最初三句，又分二科；第一科別釋相，各別解釋這三句的相貌，又分三科；第一科於諸父母等所守護，有父母等長輩所守護的，又分五科；第一科父母守護，有父母所守護的女子。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於諸父母等所守護者，猶如父母於己處女，為適事他故，勤加守護，時時觀察，不令與餘共為鄙穢。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　各個父母等長輩所守護的對象，猶如父母對於自己的處女（女孩子），為了要將她嫁給適當的對象，來奉侍所嫁的男子，努力精勤加以守護，時常觀察，不讓所守護的女孩子跟他人做不清淨的事情。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、至親守護</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科至親守護，由具血緣的至親兄弟姊妹守護。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若彼沒已，復為至親兄弟姊妹之所守護。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果女孩子的父母已經不在世間，接著是由她的兄弟姊妹所保護。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、餘親守護</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科餘親守護，則由較遠的親屬守護。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此若無者，復為餘親之所守護。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若沒有兄弟姊妹，可能就是給其他的堂兄弟，表兄弟等所保護。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地四、自己守護</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科自己守護，由自己守護自己。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此若無者，恐損家族，便自守護。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一種女孩子，沒有父母、沒有兄弟姊妹，也沒有其他的親戚朋友，為恐怕損害她家族的名譽，就自己保護自己，不做欲邪行的事情。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地五、舅姑守護</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科舅姑守護，由父母的兄弟姊妹守護。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或彼舅姑，為自兒故，勤加守護。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或是由她的舅舅或是姑姑，將她當成自己的孩子一樣，努力的來守護她，使她不受他人的侵害。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、有治罰</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有治罰，由有管理執法者的守護。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p591"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">有治罰者，謂諸國王，若執理者，以治罰法而守護故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有治罰，是指有國家的法令，有執法者，如國王、大臣、或法官、警察等，由法律及執法的人來保護未出嫁的女子。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天三、有障礙</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科有障礙，指有看管進出守門者的障礙。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">有障礙者，謂守門者所守護故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有障礙，是指未出嫁的女子居住的地方有守門的人，在那裡守護她，使得他人不易去侵害她，這是說到三種情況。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、略顯義</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科略顯義，要略顯示其中的義理。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="48090:5779"></a>此中略顯未適他者三種守護。一、尊重至親眷屬自己之所守護，二、王執理家之所守護，三、諸守門者之所守護。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處要略顯示，還沒有出嫁的女子，被三種人所保護。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、父母尊重及兄弟姐妹至親、其他的親戚朋友眷屬、或者是自己保護；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、王執理家之所守護，國王，法令，或者是法官所保護；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、諸守門者之所守護，居住的地方有守門的人來保護。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、後七句7　亥一、他妻妾</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科後七句，以後七句說明欲邪行，又分七科；第一科他妻妾，他人的妻妾。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">他妻妾者，謂已適他。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　已經嫁給他人的女人，不可以侵害她。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、他所攝</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科他所攝，屬於他人所攝的女子。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">他所攝者，謂即未適他，為三守護之所守護。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　他所攝的，還沒有嫁給他人的女子，有前面所說三種人守護的。有尊重至親眷屬或自己所守護、有王執理家的守護、或者諸守門者所守護的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、由凶詐</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科由凶詐，以凶惡、詐術施行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若由凶詐者，謂矯亂已而行邪行。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是用凶惡、詐術方法，以矯亂、欺騙、混亂女子的心，可能是給她下藥或者是用其他方法來欺騙女子，而行邪行，也是不可以的，</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂矯亂已而行邪行者：矯設方法令彼惑亂，如行誑諂等，是名矯亂。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以詐術設計很多方法，使令女子被迷惑，心裡慌亂，例如以謊言欺騙，或者是以諂媚語，對其行邪行，名為矯亂。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p592"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥四、由彊力</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科由彊力，用威脅強迫的力量。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若由彊力者，謂對父母等公然彊逼。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是用威脅強迫的力量，有一種是逼婚的情況，有些人勢力比較大，對女孩子的父母公然逼迫，威脅對方將女兒嫁給他，這都算在欲邪行裡面。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥五、由隱伏</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科由隱伏，指男女互相隱藏彼此欣欲的事。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若由隱伏者，謂不對彼，竊相欣欲。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若由隱伏，沒有對父母說，男女互相的，偷偷的做欲邪行的事。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂不對彼竊相欣欲者：此不對彼，謂不對彼父母等公然彊逼，唯由隱竊，互相欣欲。為簡公顯，故作是說。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的不對彼，指不對女子父母等公然威脅強迫，只是私底下男女互相欣欲。為了簡別公開明顯逼迫，因此這樣說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥六、行欲行</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科行欲行，說明行欲行的相貌。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">而行欲行者，謂兩兩交會。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　行欲行，是男女兩兩交會的欲行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂兩兩交會者：由二補特伽羅及彼男女二根展轉交會，是名兩兩交會。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　兩兩交會，是由二個人在一起，由男女根和合展轉交會，名為兩兩交會。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥七、即於此事非理欲心而行邪行</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科即於此事非理欲心而行邪行，以不如理的欲心，行不如理的欲邪行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即於此事非理欲心而行邪行者，謂於非道、非處、非時，自妻妾所而為罪失。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於此男女和合事，以不如理的欲心而行邪行的，是指於不是女方的產門、不是適當的處所、不是適當的時間，即使是對自己的妻妾這樣做，也是有罪業與過失的。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p593"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂於非道非處等者：此中非道，亦名非支，謂除產門外所有餘分。若諸尊重所集會處，或靈廟中，或大眾前，或堅硬地高下不平令不安隱，如是等處說名非處。若穢下時、胎圓滿時、飲兒乳時、受齋戒時，或有病時，謂所有病匪宜習欲，是名非時。如下決擇分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/59.htm#5799:48093">陵本五十九卷十六頁4839</a>）如是一切皆名非理，於自妻妾隨一而行，亦名欲邪行罪。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的非道，也稱為非支，是指除女方產門以外，身上任何其他的地方。非處，是指在各種尊重所集會的處所，或在靈廟中，或在大眾前，或在堅硬的地上或高低不平的地方，使令不安隱，這些處所都名為非處。若是於女方來月經時、懷孕中的胎兒已足月圓滿時、餵兒母乳時、受齋持戒時，或身體有病時，也就是所有不適合行欲行的時候，名為非時。在〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷59，1962頁也有說到這件事。這裡一切所說的都稱為非理，即使對於自己的妻妾中任一人有這種欲行，也都名為犯了欲邪行罪。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、明略義</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明略義，說明要略的義理。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中略義者，謂略顯示若彼所行、若行差別、若欲邪行應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這其中要略的義理，是要略顯示所做的行為、所做行為的差別、及屬於欲邪行的行為，應該要知道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此中略義等者：若彼所行，配屬別句中前五句。若行差別，配屬次三句。若欲邪行，配屬後二句應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這十句話可以再將它歸納成三類來說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一類：若彼所行，配屬別句中前五句的：一、於諸父母等所守護，二、有治罰，有法律的守護，三、是有障礙，四、是他妻妾，五、是他所攝。若對這樣的對象有邪行，稱為欲邪行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二類：行差別，配屬次三句，一、由凶詐，二、由彊力，強迫，強迫的方式，三、由隱伏，私底下的。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三類：若欲邪行，配屬後二句，包括一、行邪行，二、與即於此事非理欲心而行邪行。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、妄語2　申一、總句</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科妄語，說明妄語者的相貌，分二科；第一科總句，總說句。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，諸妄語者者，此是總句。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，說妄語的人這件事，這是總說句。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、別句2　酉一、釋經句9　戌一、於王家</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別句，各別解釋妄語者的相貌，分二科；第一科釋經句，解釋經中的文句，又分九科；第一科於王家，在國王的處所。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若王者，謂王家。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若王，在國王那裡說妄語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、於執理家</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科於執理家，在執行公務者的處所。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若彼使者，謂執理家。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若彼使，替國王做事，執行公務、法令的公務人員，都可以稱作執理家。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p594"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、於長者居士</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科於長者居士，對長者居士。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若別者，謂長者居士。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　別者，或者說在長者居士那裡。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、於彼聚集</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科於彼聚集，於大眾聚集處所。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若眾者，謂彼聚集。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若眾，是指大眾聚集處。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌五、於四方人眾聚集處</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科於四方人眾聚集處，於來自於各方人士的聚集處。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="13017:5815"></a>若大集中者，謂四方人眾聚集處。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是大集中的，是指四方的人眾聚集在一起的處所。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌六、於已知</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科於已知，對於已知的事。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若已知者，謂隨前三所經語言。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是已知的，是指在前三，包括在王家和執理家、長者居士、聚集處所的大眾前說過，他們已經知道，稱為已知者。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂隨前三所經語言者：謂隨前時聞、覺、知三所曾經事，覆真實想而說異語，謂為已知。非唯依知言說，名為已知。義寬廣故。四言說中不言依見言說者，下別說故。四種言說，如前意地釋。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/02.htm#5818:1637">陵本二卷十九頁175</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　指在前一段時間，在王家和執理家、長者居士、聚集處所的大眾之前，隨所聽聞、覺察、了知，三種所曾經了知的事，為了隱覆內心的真實想而說與事實相反的話語，稱為已知。並不是只按照所了知的言說出來，名為已知。從所說的話，由說的不同的角度、所說的深淺，可知所說的不是真實語，不是真實語的範圍是很寬廣的。見、聞、覺、知四種言說中，沒有說依見言說，下面會另外別說。四種言說，如同前〈意地〉卷2， 75頁所解釋的可知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌七、於已見</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科於已見，於已曾經見過的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若已見者，謂隨曾見所經語言。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若已見，隨曾看到的境相而說妄語，稱為已見。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p595"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌八、由自因等2　亥一、略標2　天一、舉由自因</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科由自因等，說妄語二種的原因，分二科；第一科略標，要略標示出，又分二科；第一科舉由自因，舉出由自己的原因。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若由自因者，謂或因怖畏，或因味著。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是由自己的原因，或是由於自己害怕，如果說真實話會受到迫害、對自己不利，或是因為愛味染著，喜歡說謊話。不只說謊話會成為習慣，殺盜淫妄通通都會習慣的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、例由他因</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例由他因，舉出由他人的原因說妄語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如由自因，他因亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如同由於自己的原因說妄語，由他人的原因也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》如由自因他因亦爾者：由自怖畏，或自味著，名由自因；如前已說。或復由他怖畏，由他味著，教敕令作，名由他因；故言亦爾。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於自己害怕，或者因為自己愛味染著說謊，名為由自因，如前已說。或是由於他人的原因，若說實話心裡會有所怖畏，或是由他因愛味染著妄語事，而教唆使令自己說妄語，名為由他因。因此說由他因也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、別釋2　天一、因怖畏</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋，各別的解釋，分二科；第一科因怖畏，因恐怖畏懼而說妄語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">因怖畏者，謂由怖畏殺、縛、治罰、黜責等故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因恐怖畏懼而說妄語，因為害怕若說實語，對方會殺他、綁他、處罰他、或者是受到罷黜驅擯的責罰等，感到怖畏說妄語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、因味著</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科因味著，因愛味染著而說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">因味著者，謂為財穀、珍寶等故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為愛味染著，為貪著財穀，珍寶等，怕如果說出實話會得不到。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌九、知而說妄語</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科知而說妄語，隱藏所想、所欲、己見而說妄語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">知而說妄語者，謂覆想欲見而說語言。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　知而說妄語，是指為了隱藏自己的想法、心中所欲、自己執著的見而說的語言。覆，是隱藏心裡的想法；欲，是心裡的好樂、願望，這樣想卻那樣說，或是喜歡這樣說，卻不想這樣說，說出另外一套。見，是自己的一種思想理論，想久了變成一套固定的思想，稱為「見」，說的話與自己的見不同，口是心非。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p596"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》覆想欲見而說語言者：心所取相，是名為想；心所樂欲，是名為欲；心所忍可，是名為見。由此三故能起語言。諸妄語者說別異語，令真不顯，是名為覆。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　接觸境界時，心依名言取相，稱為想；心所樂欲，內心歡喜好樂，說名為欲；心所忍可，對所認知的事達到忍可的程度，有決定性的認識，是名為見。由於有想、有欲、有見能發起語言說話。說妄語的人，將真實隱藏起來，說出與真實事不同的異語，使令真實相不顯現，是名為覆。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、明略義</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明略義，說明要略的義理。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中略義者，謂依處故、異說故、因緣故、壞想故，而說妄語應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其中的要義，包括：依處、異說、因緣、壞想，四種原因而說妄語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此中略義等者：依處故，配屬別句中若王等五句。異說故，配屬已知已見二句。因緣故，配屬自因他因等句。壞想故，配屬知而覆妄語句應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　要略的義理中，依處，配屬別句中的王家、執理家、長者居士、眾者、四方眾聚集處等五句。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　異說，配屬已知已見二句的已知覆真實說異語。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因緣，配屬自因他因的怖畏、味著等句。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　壞想，配屬知而覆想欲見而說妄語句，應該要了知。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是十不善業，分析妄語者的相貌，在哪裡說，為什麼會說妄語，不外是經過見聞覺知，因緣是自己害怕，或者是味著財物，或者是因為他人。知而說妄語，或為隱藏真實的想、欲、見，說出妄語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未五、離間語攝2　申一、總句</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科離間語攝，說明離間語者所攝的相貌，分二科；第一科總句，總說句。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="29077:5839"></a>復次，離間語者者，此是總句。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，說離間語的人這件事，這是總說句。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、別句2　酉一、釋經句7　戌一、若為破壞</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別句，各別說明離間語的相貌，分二科；第一科釋經句，解釋經中的文句與義理，又分七科；第一科若為破壞，為破壞而說離間語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若為破壞者，謂由破壞意樂故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若是為破壞的目的，指內心有要破壞對方的意樂，才說離間語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、聞彼語已向此宣說等</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科聞彼語已向此宣說等，隨所聽聞而說離間語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">聞彼語已向此宣說，聞此語已向彼宣說者，謂隨所聞順乖離語。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　離間語表達的方式，是從甲聽到所說後，向乙宣說，從乙聽到所說後，向甲宣說的人，由所聽到甲乙彼此各別所說的話中，隨順說出其中會使甲乙乖離不和的話語。也就是只說會使雙方乖離的話，而沒有說彼此間互相讚美的話，就會形成離間語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》聞彼語已向此宣說等者：謂聞彼語，或聞此語，若順乖離，則便向此、向彼而為宣說故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　聽聞到某甲的話，或者是聽到某乙的說話，如果是其中有隨順可破壞他們感情的話語，向不同的對方轉述。離間語的相貌是這樣。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p597"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌三、破壞和合</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科破壞和合，為破壞和合而說離間語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">破壞和合者，謂能生起喜別離故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　破壞和合是：使用方法讓被離間的人生起歡喜別離的願望之心念。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》破壞和合等者：謂以方便令此或彼生起不和合欲，而生別離喜故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　破壞和合的意思：是用方法使令甲與乙生起不和合的願望，而生起歡喜彼此別離的心。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌四、隨印別離</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科隨印別離，隨順印可他人的別離而說離間語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">隨印別離者，謂能乖違喜更生故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　隨順印可他人的分離，遂使他人乖違不合而分開的歡喜心能夠再生起。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》隨印別離等者：謂以方便印順彼別離喜，從是乖違喜不更生故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以離間語的方法，隨順印可他人分離而生起的歡喜，由於他人彼此乖違不順而生的歡喜心己不再生起了。隨印別離可令之再起。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌五、喜壞和合</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科喜壞和合，歡喜破壞和合而說離間語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">喜壞和合者，謂於已生喜別離中心染汙故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　喜歡破壞和合，指對於看到他人心中已經生起歡喜別離的心，此時說離間語者感覺快樂，心為煩惱所染污。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》喜壞和合等者：謂彼若此若已生喜別離，能離間者遂破壞欲，生染汙喜故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若看到他人彼此已歡喜要分離，能離間者達到破壞的欲望，生起有染污的歡喜心。這個是離間的染污心，前面是方法，一是用方法使對方生起歡喜要離開的心，二是讓他們能夠決定要離開，三在形容離間者內心的情況，這是一種事不同的說法，喜壞和合與破壞和合，一種是形容心相，一種是形容行動。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌六、樂印別離</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科樂印別離，樂於印可對方別離。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">樂印別離者，謂於乖違喜更生中心染汙故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　樂於印可對方別離者：是指確保所離間的對象能持續乖違而生歡喜，這時心生離間煩惱的染汙。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p598"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》樂印別離等者：謂彼若此從是乖違喜不更生，能離間者破壞意樂圓滿，而生染汙樂故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　被離間者以此持續乖違的歡喜心，能離間者的破壞意樂已經圓滿達到，而生起染汙的快樂。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌七、說能離間語</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科說能離間語，說能離間的語言。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">說能離間語者，謂或不聞，或他方便故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此指其他能成辦的能離間語。例如，當離間者聽到所要離間對象彼此讚歎對方，卻裝做沒有聽到，因為不去勸和，也算是能離間語的另外一種方便。或是離間者不自己說，透過第三者去成辦間接的能離間語。前面六科都是直接說能離間語。此科是透過其他的方法，來成辦能離間語者。這是《披尋記》的解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　玅境長老說的是另外一種解釋：某甲及某乙聽到離間者的離間語，可是沒有將它聽進去，使得能離間者說的沒有成功，稱為謂或不聞。或者能離間者用其他的方法，而沒有成功。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》說能離間語等者：謂若此語能令乖離，是則此語名能離間。如聞彼此順乖離語，則向此彼展轉宣說。如是宣說，當知名為能離間語。如前已說。今此更顯由他方便，為乖離彼而有所說，亦名能離間語。如聞彼此順和合語，則向此彼謂為不聞。或復依止親近、施與、知友、給侍以為方便而有陳說，皆名能離間語。如下決擇分說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/59.htm#5861:48116">陵本五十九卷十七頁4841</a>）</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所說的話使令對方能夠互相違背而離開，這種話名為能離間。例如聽聞到某甲或某乙所說隨順乖離的語言，離間者就向某乙或某甲宣說所聽到的乖離語，所轉述的話，名為能離間語。前面第一科到第六科所說的都是直接說能離間語。第七科說的能離間語，顯示由其他的方法為使他們分開，而有所說，雖然不是自己說，或者用其他的方法，也名為能離間語。例如聽聞彼此互相隨順和合的語言，則向此彼說不曾聽過，或透過親近、布施對方的人、對方的知心好友、侍奉對方的人以為方便而有所說，都名為能離間語。如下〈決擇‧有尋有伺等三地〉卷59，1966頁裡面也說到這件事。謂為不聞，在大正藏經窺基大師也有一種解釋，不聞就是對方聽不懂，因此離間沒有成功。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、明略義</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明略義，說明要略的義理。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p599"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中略義者，謂略顯示離間意樂、離間未壞方便、離間已壞方便、離間染汙心，及他方便應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其中的要義，要略顯示離間意樂、離間未壞方便、離間已壞方便、離間染汙心，及他方便五項應當了知。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此中略義等者：離間意樂，配屬別句中若為破壞句。離間未壞方便，配屬聞彼語已至向彼宣說句。離間已壞方便，配屬破壞和合及隨印別離句。離間染汙心，配屬喜壞和合及樂印別離句。他方便，配屬說能離間語句應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　要略分成五項來說明離間句的配屬：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、離間意樂：配屬若為破壞；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、離間未壞方便：配屬聞彼語已向此宣說；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、離間已壞方便：配屬破壞和合、隨印別離；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、離間染污心：配屬喜壞和合、樂印別離；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、他方便：配屬說能離間語。以上是說離間語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未六、麤惡語攝2　申一、總句</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科麤惡語攝，說明麤惡語者所攝的相貌，分二科；第一科總句，總說句。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，麤惡語者者，此是總句。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，說麤惡語者的事，這是總說句。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、別句2　酉一、舉相違2　戌一、釋經句12　亥一、語無擾動</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別句，各別說的句子，又分二科；第一科舉相違，從反面來說麤惡語，又分二科；第一科釋經句，解釋經中所說，又分十二科；第一科語無擾動，說話不擾動人心。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　本論在十種不善業中，唯有在麤惡語這裡是以反面的說法介紹，主要是基於本論為大乘的菩薩藏，菩薩留惑潤生，不入涅槃而發心在五濁惡世濟度眾生，處污泥中而不染，更不會造十惡業，所有對眾生說的話語，都是為眾生現前與將來的利益為出發點，因此所說的話，都是如法的、符合戒律的、使令眾生平等歡喜的、易可解了的。在這一大科中會詳細介紹菩薩所說的話語，可歸納為：語無擾動、悅耳、稱心、可愛、先首、美妙、分明、易可解了、可施功勞、無所依止、非可厭逆、無邊無盡等十二種，又可歸納為：尸羅律儀所攝語、等歡喜語、說法語，及可愛可樂可欣可意語、三摩呬多語等。下面會逐一詳細介紹，使得佛弟子們在警惕自己勿以煩惱造業外，更要學習在善法中菩薩所說的種種利益眾生的話語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中尸羅支所攝故，名語無擾動。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有受持戒律所說的話，說話時不會擾亂他人的心，稱為語無擾動。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》語無擾動者：謂無憤發掉舉及躁急掉舉故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於有受持戒律，心情平靜，所說的話平穩安和，沒有情緒波動、沒有躁動急切不安的情形。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、悅耳</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科悅耳，好聽的話。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">文句美滑，故名悅耳。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　文句美滑，所說的話輕易柔和，能使聽聞者獲得利益安樂，名為悅耳。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》文句美滑等者：言不鄙陋，是名為美。言皆輕易，是名為滑。眾樂聽聞，故名悅耳。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所說的話不是很粗陋或是很下劣的語言，是比較文雅的話，名為美。所說的話輕易柔和，容易領受，使得眾人都很喜歡聽，名為悅耳。這唯有佛才能夠完全做到。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥三、稱心</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科稱心，稱合心意的話。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p600"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">增上欲解所發起故，非假偽故，非諂媚故，名為稱心。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由強而有力的認識與深刻的了解所發起的，是真實的，不是虛假的，也不是為討好、巴結、奉承，說好聽的話，名為稱心。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》增上欲解至名為稱心者：謂依增上生道樂欲忍可而起言說，是名增上欲解之所發起。是諦是實，名非假偽。無諂無誑，名非諂媚。眾樂領受，故名稱心。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡所說的都是依止增上生道，心中欣欲好樂印可所發起的言說，名為增上欲解之所發起。是真實不虛的，稱為非假偽。沒有諂媚欺誑，稱為非諂媚。大家都歡喜領受，故名稱心。說法使令能夠布施，持戒，修福，到人天受生，一生比一生更好，名為增上生道。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥四、可愛</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科可愛，令人喜愛能引義利的話。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不增益故，應順時機，引義利故，名為可愛。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所說的話，如其所應有的量，不擅自增加，能隨順相應適當的時間，與適應聽者的根機，能引發現前與將來的義利，名為可愛。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》不增益故至名為可愛者：如實而說，名不增益。應時而說，順眾而說，如法而說，是名應順時機及引義利。順往善趣，故名可愛。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如事實的真相、如其所應有的量來說，名為不增益。隨順適當的時間與當時在場眾生的根器而說，如佛所說的法來說，名為應順時機及引義利。這樣說法，使令聽者能隨順得到人天善趣的樂果，名為可愛。稱心跟可愛都屬於增上生道，勸他人修五戒十善的話語，是稱心的是可愛的，可使有情到人天的善趣受果。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥五、先首</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科先首，以涅槃為上首。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="32178:5882"></a><a name="61994:5882"></a><a name="34667:5882"></a>趣涅槃宮，故名先首。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所說的話有引導人朝向涅槃去的功能，名為先首。涅槃宮是沒有貪瞋癡的地方，是修行人究竟要達到的目標，名為先首。說法應以涅槃為上首。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》趣涅槃宮故名先首者：謂說法者為令眾生越生死塹，故所說法唯以趣涅槃宮為其上首，令彼眾生起勝意樂，趣涅槃故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說法人的動機，是要讓眾生超越生死的溝塹，因此所說的法都是引領眾生趣涅槃宮為其上首，使得眾生發起殊勝的意樂，趣向涅槃。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥六、美妙</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科美妙，語言美好微妙。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p601"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">文句可味，故名美妙。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說法者說法的內容很可味，令人生喜生樂，很可愛味，名為美妙。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》文句可味故名美妙者：其聲清美，如羯羅頻迦音故。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說話的聲音非常的清澈，非常的美好，好像羯羅頻迦鳥發出來的聲音，聽了就很舒適，很美妙。文句可味，聲音是清澈明亮，美好的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥七、分明</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科分明，說話清楚明白。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">善釋文句，故名分明。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所說的話，能夠很圓滿、很完整，明明白白的解釋文句的義理，因此名為分明。說話非常有條理，非常明白，一聽就懂，這也是如理如法的特徵。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥八、易可解了</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科易可解了，容易了解。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">顯然有趣，故名易可解了。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所說的話，直接聽就懂了，是明顯的，有趣的，能引起愛樂聽聞的動機，名為易可解了。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》顯然有趣故名易可解了者：言無闕隱，是名顯然。愛樂聽聞，是名有趣。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所說的話，沒有缺少，也沒有隱藏，名為顯然。說的法語，能使對方愛樂聽聞，名為有趣。總之說的不會讓對方睡著，說的話也能引起聽眾好樂聽聞。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥九、可施功勞</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科可施功勞，對修行有實際的幫助，能攝受正法。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">攝受正法，故名可施功勞。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　玅境長老解釋聖者離言說的第一義諦，稱為正法。成就第一義諦必須攝受正法，就是要修止修觀，或者是念佛，透過修行才能夠攝受正法，才能與法相應。所說的話，能使令聽聞正法的人能夠去修行，這樣做一定沒有錯，決定可以到達聖道那裡。換言之所說的話，可以依之修行聖道，證悟第一義諦，名為可施功勞。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》攝受正法等者：聽聞正法，如說修行，能引自義，功不唐捐，故名可施功勞。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依聽聞正法，能夠如所說的來修行，能夠引生成就涅槃聖道的功德，所投入的功夫不會白白的浪費，名為可施功勞。能引自義，義就是涅槃。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥十、無所依止</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科無所依止，無染著心而說。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">離愛味心之所發起，故名無所依止。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說法人的心情必須是清淨的，不是為了名聞利養，也不是要諂媚對方，或者是要爭取自己的利益來說法，說法人的動機是以無所得的大慈悲心而說，名為無所依止。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p602"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》離愛味心至無所依止者：不依希望他信己故而為說法，名離愛味心之所發起。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說法的人，不是為了希望聽法的人相信自己而說法，名為離愛味心之所發起。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥十一、非可厭逆</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科非可厭逆，言語不使人厭惡違逆。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不過度量，故名非可厭逆。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所說的話適當、不超過度量，名為非可厭逆。語多人就嫌煩，眾生也很怕煩的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》不過度量等者：知量而說，語無重複，是名不過度量。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　能夠知量而說，所說的話沒有重複，名為不過度量。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥十二、無邊無盡</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科無邊無盡，言語及義理無邊無盡。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">相續廣大，故名無邊無盡。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　善說法的人，所說的法語，是相續廣大的，法味法義是無邊無盡的。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》相續廣大等者：言辭無間，廣大善巧，是名相續廣大。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　善說法的人，所說的法語言辭流暢、沒有間斷，而且很廣大，很善巧，可以說出法語裡面深刻的義理，聽者事後還會回味無窮，是名相續廣大。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、略明攝2　亥一、初三種2　天一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科略明攝，說明六種所攝，分二科；第一科初三種，最初三種，分二科；第一科標，標出三種。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又從無擾動語乃至無邊無盡語，應知略攝為三種語。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所說的話語，從無擾動語乃至無邊無盡語十二種，應知要略可以歸納成三種語言。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、列3　地一、尸羅律儀所攝語</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列舉出來，分三科；第一科尸羅律儀所攝語，由戒律所攝的語言。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、尸羅律儀所攝語，謂一種。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三種語的第一種，尸羅律儀所攝語，是指前面的語無擾動，如果持戒的話，所說的話不會攪亂他人平靜的心情。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、等歡喜語</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科等歡喜語，平等歡喜的語言。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p603"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、等歡喜語，謂三種。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三種語的第二種，等歡喜語，使眾人平等歡喜的語言，分三種：悅耳、稱心、可愛。說話時使人喜歡聽，文句美華，名悅耳；說話時使人修五戒十善能得增上生道，名稱心。說話時能夠順應時機，利義對方，不增益故，名為可愛。這三句，名為等歡喜語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地三、說法語2　玄一、標攝</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科說法語，說法的語言。分二科；第一科標攝，標示出所攝的內容。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、說法語，謂其所餘。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三種語的第三種說法語，是指十二種語言中的後八種。由先首開始一直到無邊無際，都稱為說法語，說法語必須要達到這個標準。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》略攝為三種語等者：最初一種語無擾動，名尸羅律儀所攝語。次三悅耳、稱心、可愛，名等歡喜語；等遍三世無量眾生樂聽聞故。所餘八種，先首乃至無邊無盡，名說法語。前說增上生道，此說決定勝道，是故有別。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十二種語言要略攝為三種，最初一種：語無擾動，名為尸羅律儀所攝語。次三種語：悅耳、稱心、可愛，名為等歡喜語，「等」字，是指遍於去今來三世無量的眾生都會愛樂聽聞。所餘的八種語，先首乃至無邊無盡，名為說法語。前面四種所說的：語無擾動、悅耳、稱心、可愛，是可以使得一生比一生增上的增上生道。所餘的八種語：先首、美妙、分明、易可解了、可施功勞、無所依止、非可厭逆、無邊無盡，是可以解脫三界，成就聖道的決定勝道，因此有所差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、別廣2　黃一、標</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別廣，各別廣泛的解釋，分二科；第一科標，標出三種。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即此最後又有三種應知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此，是指說法語，說法語共有八句，又可以分成三種。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">黃二、列3　宇一、所趣圓滿語</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三種，分三科；第一科所趣圓滿語，所趣向圓滿的語言。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、所趣圓滿語，謂初一。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所趣圓滿語，指第一句先首，以趣涅槃宮為先首，使令所趣圓滿。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇二、文詞圓滿語</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科文詞圓滿語，文詞圓滿的語言。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二、文詞圓滿語，謂次二。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　文詞圓滿語，指第二美妙、第三句分明。文詞圓滿法語，能使聽者易於領受。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">宇三、方便圓滿語</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科方便圓滿語，方便圓滿的語言。</span></span></span></div>
<a name="08p604"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三、方便圓滿語，謂其所餘。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　方便圓滿語，指第四～八句：易可解了、可施功勞、無所依止、非可厭逆、無邊無盡。方便圓滿語，可使聽者依種種所教導的方便修行，成就聖道。說法人的智慧很高，善巧方便，透過這樣的語言，可使人到達涅槃的彼岸。這樣的語言是非常的圓滿，名為方便圓滿語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》即此最後又有三種等者：謂說法語又有三種差別，如文易知。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　說法語，像文所說的很容易明白，包括：所趣圓滿語、文詞圓滿語、方便圓滿語三種差別。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">亥二、後三種3　天一、無量眾生可愛可樂可欣可意語2　地一、別釋3　玄一、可愛語</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科後三種，說明後三種，分三科；第一科無量眾生可愛可樂可欣可意語，無量眾生都喜歡聽的可愛話語，又分二科；第一科別釋，各別的解釋，又分三科；第一科可愛語，可使人愛樂聽聞的語言。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於未來世可愛樂故，名可愛語。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷2說：「謂未來諸佛當說十二種妙語名可愛語。過去諸佛曾說名可樂語。現在諸佛今說及正領受生他愛樂名可欣語可意語。」十二句妙語，是指無擾動語、悅耳語、稱心語、可愛語、先首語、美妙語、分明語、易可解了語、可施功勞語、無所依止語、非可厭逆語、無邊無盡語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄二、可樂語</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科可樂語，可使聽聞者歡喜愛樂的語言。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於過去世可愛樂故，名可樂語。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷2說：「過去諸佛曾說十二種妙語，名可樂語。」</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">玄三、可欣及可意語</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科可欣及可意語，可使聽聞者欣喜適意的語言。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於現在世事及領受可愛樂故，名可欣語及可意語。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷2說：「現在諸佛今說十二種妙語及正領受生其他有情愛樂名可欣語、可意語。」&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">地二、結攝</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結攝，結說所含攝的義理。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">應知即等歡喜語，名無量眾生可愛、可樂、可欣、可意語。</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應該知道這就是悅耳語，即前三語中第二等歡喜語，包括悅耳語、稱心語、可愛語，名為無量眾生可愛、可樂、可欣、可意語。這是前三種語中的第二種語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">天二、三摩呬多語</span></strong></span></span>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科三摩呬多語，即說法語。</span></span></span></div>
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">即說法語，名三摩呬多語。</span></strong></span></span>
